    <h1 id="title">
     <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/">
      <span>
       Escape From New York
      </span>
     </a>
    </h1>
    <p id="description">
     Tracey's Travels
    </p>
   </div>
   <div id="wrapper_inner">
    <div id="center">
     <div id="blogcontent">
      <div class="entry">
       <h2 class="entrytitle" id="Entry110">
        <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/110/" rel="bookmark" title="Permanent link to A Weekend in Charleston: I've Got Friends in Low Places ">
         A Weekend in Charleston: I've Got Friends in Low Places
        </a>
       </h2>
       <p class="preentrydetails">
        <span class="entrydate">
         05.14.2015
        </span>
       </p>
       <div class="entrycontent">
        <p>
         "Wow, that's, um, er, . . .
         <em>
          adventurous
         </em>
         .  You'll enable the GPS on your phone just in case, though, right?"
        </p>
        <p>
         That was the general consensus when I told some friends that I was planning to spend President's Day weekend in Charleston's Low Country with a woman named Sue, whom I'd never met.
        </p>
        <p>
         And that our accommodations for the weekend would be provided by Sue's friend Missy, whom I'd never met, either.
        </p>
        <p>
         Of course, I don't usually recommend jumping on a plane to meet up with strangers you find on the Internet, but when the offer includes a free beach house and a three-day binge on pig parts and punch bowls, you'd be crazy to say no.
        </p>
        <p>
         Or at least just crazy.
        </p>
        <p>
         Sue and I became acquainted online a few years ago after I wrote
         <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/44/">
          a three-part blog post about my food-filled weekend in Charleston
         </a>
         , where she lived for nearly 20 years before moving to North Carolina in 2013 to care for her aging mother.   We bonded over a mutual love of everything from fried chicken skins to watermelon martinis, communicating online about food, travel, and where we might travel next for some food.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Aerial1_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Aerial1_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         That turned out to be Charleston, thanks to Sue's friend Missy, who generously offered us the use of her beach house on Sullivan's Island for a long weekend.  Weeks of obsessive planning about where and what to eat and drink ensued, with menus and cocktail lists whizzing through cyberspace while Sue and I  bombarded each other's inboxes with photos of pork chops, cheese grits, and bourbon drinks.  Which sure beats the usual contents of my inbox, which usually consists of the secrets to enlarging certain parts of my body and shrinking others.
        </p>
        <p>
         Finally, the appointed weekend arrived. Sue drove down from Greensboro and I flew down from New York, and in the 20 minutes it took to drive from the airport into downtown Charleston, Sue and I had already decided to pace ourselves for not one but two lunches and were debating about a snack in between.  How could I
         <em>
          not
         </em>
         like her?
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Amen_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Amen_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We parked the car and ambled in the sunshine over to Amen Street Fish &amp; Raw Bar, which was one of the spots I ran out of time for on my last visit.  (Hence the two-lunches-a-day schedule this time around.  Live and learn.)
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Amen1_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Amen1_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Amen_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Amen_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Famed for its gorgeous oyster-shell chandeliers, Amen Street is bustling and bright, and we were happy to discover that we'd arrived just in time to avoid the one-lunch crowd.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Amen_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Amen_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Amen2_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Amen2_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_rawbar_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_rawbar_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         I knew had to try the "Owner's Famous Frozen Peach Bellini," which is made with both Champagne and rum.  If one lunch would not suffice, you can bet only one booze wouldn't.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_AmenMimosa_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_AmenMimosa_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Sue went with the Bloody Mary, which she loved.  Me, I don't like a lot of random vegetables coming between me and my liquor.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Amen_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Amen_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Amen_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Amen_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Amen_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Amen_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         You know what's better than a corn dog?
        </p>
        <p>
         That's a trick question: Nothing is better than a corn dog.  But a
         <em>
          shrimp
         </em>
         corn dog comes pretty close.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Amen_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Amen_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Amen_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Amen_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Amen_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Amen_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We also split an order of shrimp ceviche and a third drink, the Chef's Old Fashioned, with bourbon, muddled orange, and brandied cherries.  Of course, we didn't really
         <em>
          need
         </em>
         a third drink, but I'm pretty sure all the rules go out the window when you find yourself eating corn dogs at 11am with someone you just met an hour ago.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Amen_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Amen_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Amen_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Amen_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         After lunch we milled around for a bit, taking in the sights and enjoying the warm sun on our faces.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Arrival_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Arrival_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Arrival_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Arrival_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_CHSsights_22.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_CHSsights_22.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Arrival_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Arrival_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Arrival_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Arrival_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_Arrival2_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_Arrival2_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Amen_20.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Amen_20.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Arrival_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Arrival_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Arrival_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Arrival_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_34.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_34.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_36.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_36.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Arrival_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Arrival_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_CHSsights_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_CHSsights_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Arrival_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Arrival_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Arrival_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Arrival_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Arrival_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Arrival_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Arrival_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Arrival_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_Arrival_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_Arrival_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Soon, however, it was time for lunch.  Again.  And so off we went to the Obstinate Daughter on Sullivan's Island.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Sullivan_8.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Sullivan_8.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_Sullivan_6.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_Sullivan_6.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_OD_26.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_OD_26.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_OD_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_OD_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_OD_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_OD_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_OD_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_OD_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The restaurant's unusual name is an homage to the Battle of Sullivan's Island during the Revolutionary War, in which the defenders of Fort Sullivan foiled the British fleets attempt to capture the city of Charleston. This first American Patriots victory inspired a London political cartoon of Miss Carolina Sullivan, one of the "obstinate daughters of America," whose large hairdo concealed fortifications, cannons, and battle flags.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_OD_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_OD_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The restaurant's web site notes, "To us, the Obstinate Daughter is a beautiful reminder that the stubborn refusal to change ones course of action can change the course of history."
        </p>
        <p>
         That is true.  Because, although we were still plenty full from our corn dogs and cocktails at Amen Street, we forged ahead with our planned course of action.  Onward, soldiers! The mighty cannot be felled, neither by gluttony nor by gout!
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_OD_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_OD_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_OD_20.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_OD_20.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_OD_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_OD_17.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_OD_24.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_OD_24.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The O/D, as it's called, was until recently a beloved Sullivan's Island institution called Atlanticville, which was one of Sue's favorite haunts.  So she was understandably a bit leery about giving the O/D a try.   But I don't think she had anything to worry about.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_OD_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_OD_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_OD_21.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_OD_21.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_OD_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_OD_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_OD_25.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_OD_25.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Although it was mid-afternoon, the place was pretty busy, so instead of waiting for a table, we decided to grab two seats at the bar.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_OD_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_OD_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_OD_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_OD_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         After a short bout of indecision, Sue settled on the Low Country shrimp roll with tasty little fried polenta sticks called "geechie fries," which she paired with the Swamp Fox cocktail.  Made with bourbon, maple syrup, Luxardo cherry liqueur, Fresno chilies, and bitters, the Swamp Fox probably should have tasted like that vile cayenne-pepper lemonade people drink to lose weight, but instead tasted like the kind of well-made, sophisticated cocktail people drink to wash down their second lunch of the day.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_OD_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_OD_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_OD_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_OD_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         After finding myself unable to tear my eyes (and just barely my fork) away from my neighbor's delicious-looking entre, I ordered the same thing: Homemade gnocchi with short rib ragu, horseradish, and pine nut gremolata.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_OD_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_OD_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Although nearly everything on the O/D's cocktail list sounded amazing, I went with the Palmetto Log Colada, which started off traditional with rum, pineapple, and coconut milk, then veered into interesting with the addition of crushed ice and a sweet surprise: blueberry honey.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_OD_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_OD_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We'd just finished eating when another patron ordered this:
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_OD_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_OD_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         That is a sticky bun with caramel and pecans.  Have you ever seen anyone actually make a sticky bun?  It's like spreading an oil tanker full of butter onto half a slice of toast.  But after shrimp corn dogs and short rib gnocchi, what's 10,000 more calories?  The bartender told us it was too late in the day to order one, but I think the look on my face made it clear that he had two choices: Get the kitchen to make me a sticky bun, or get the manager to come and break up the fistfight I was going to start with the person who ordered the day's last sticky bun.
        </p>
        <p>
         He got me the sticky bun.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_OD_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_OD_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         That afternoon we explored Sullivan's Island a bit.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Sullivan_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Sullivan_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Sullivan_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Sullivan_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Sullivan_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Sullivan_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Sullivan_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Sullivan_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_Sullivan_7.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_Sullivan_7.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Finally, it was time to head back to what Sue referred to as "the beachiest beach house ever."  And it was.  Spacious, airy, and unfussy, the house radiated the simple charm of a lived-in beach cottage, the kind where everyone is having too good a time to fret much over sandy feet on the floors.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_house_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_house_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_house_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_house_17.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_house_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_house_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_house_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_house_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_house_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_house_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_house_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_house_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_house_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_house_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_house_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_house_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_house_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_house_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_house_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_house_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_house_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_house_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         My room was bright and cheery, with lots of fluffy towels and a warm, soft quilt on the bed.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_house_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_house_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_house_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_house_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <a class="enlarge_image" href="/image_enlarge.cfm?src=http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_house_12.jpg" onclick="raw_popup(this);return false" title="Click for full size image">
          <img alt="2015_CHS_house_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/thumb_2015_CHS_house_12.jpg"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         By the end of the day we were both too tired and too full to follow through on our original dinner plans, so Sue suggested the appropriately-named Stack's Evening Eats in nearby Mt. Pleasant for snacks and wine instead.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Stacks_6.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Stacks_6.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Stacks_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Stacks_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         There, we sat at the bar with a couple glasses of crisp white wine, a plate of fried oysters, and the best Brussels sprouts I've ever had.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Stacks_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Stacks_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Stacks_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Stacks_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Stacks_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Stacks_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Stacks_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Stacks_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The Brussels sprouts were fried till crispy, then served with a creamy, savory smoked tomato and herb dipping sauce. That might sound fancy, but in the South, "dipping sauce" is just a euphemism for "mayonnaise," much like "I'll have a side of bacon" really means, "Just bring me the whole hog, and be quick about it."
        </p>
        <p>
         Or, maybe they just call it dipping sauce because they know that's what you'll be doing with your fingers as soon as those Brussels sprouts are gone.
        </p>
        <p>
         The next day dawned cloudless and sunny, but also freezing.  And I don't mean southern-style, it's-65-degrees-where's-my-parka freezing.  I mean
         <em>
          freezing
         </em>
         -freezing:  Accounting for the wind chill, the day's high was roughly 40 degrees.  Luckily I came prepared.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Levard_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Levard_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Sue steered us to the Boulevard Diner, where we could wait for a table in the small vestibule instead of out in the cold.  After a bit of exercise to warm up, that is.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Levard_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Levard_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Levard_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Levard_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         That gave us time to peruse the menu and take in the old-school diner dcor.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Levard_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Levard_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Levard_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Levard_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Levard_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Levard_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Levard_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Levard_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Levard_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Levard_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Levard_20.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Levard_20.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         I really wanted fried pork chops, but Boulevard Diner was serving brunch.  Luckily, though, this is South Carolina, where fried pork chops at Sunday brunch are as commonplace as pacemakers at Sunday dinner.  And so I had the fried pork chops with scrambled eggs, cheese grits, and toast.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Levard_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Levard_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Levard_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Levard_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Levard_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Levard_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Sue went with a classic: shrimp and grits.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_Levard_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_Levard_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         If you're going to start the day with things like fried pork chops and cheese grits, there's no guarantee you'll make it to the
         <em>
          end
         </em>
         of the day.  So you might as well go for broke with some creamy coconut cake and a rich chocolate mocha pecan torte for dessert.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Levard_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Levard_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Levard_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Levard_17.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_Levard_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_Levard_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Levard_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Levard_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         After brunch we continued our exploration of Sullivan's Island, along with neighboring John's Island.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_Beach_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_Beach_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Beach_7.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Beach_7.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         It's not the $1,000 that gets me.  It's that extra $40, tacked on like a bad toupe.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_finesign_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_finesign_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         And forget looking out for jellyfish.  Here, the hazards include things like deep holes and marauding coyotes, which make the deadly currents seem somewhat redundant.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Beach_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Beach_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Beach_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Beach_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Worried about the land mines they probably forgot to mention, we headed inland a bit so Sue could show me the local neighborhoods.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_BeachHouses_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_BeachHouses_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_BeachHouses_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_BeachHouses_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_BeachHouses_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_BeachHouses_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="9D6689BA9ADAD924174E225A6B4BBB8A.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/9D6689BA9ADAD924174E225A6B4BBB8A.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_BeachHouses_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_BeachHouses_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_BeachHouses_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_BeachHouses_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_BeachHouses_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_BeachHouses_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_BeachHouses_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_BeachHouses_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_BeachHouses_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_BeachHouses_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Just when I started to think the houses all looked the same, a spaceship landed on this guy's lawn.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_BeachHouses_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_BeachHouses_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         His neighbors, however, refused to be outdone by some lousy flying saucer.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_BeachHouses_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_BeachHouses_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="9D65FFBAC54848465BAE14869136EC0E.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/9D65FFBAC54848465BAE14869136EC0E.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         After a little more driving around, we ended up at Vickery's on Shem Creek for an afternoon pick-me-up (and drink-me-down).
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_Vickerys_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_Vickerys_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Vickerys_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Vickerys_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Vickerys_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Vickerys_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_Vickerys_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_Vickerys_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         With its wraparound decks and outdoor bars, Vickery's is the perfect place to take in the view with a cocktail in hand.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Vickerys_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Vickerys_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Vickerys_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Vickerys_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Vickerys_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Vickerys_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Vickerys_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Vickerys_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_Vickerys_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_Vickerys_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Vickerys_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Vickerys_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Vickerys_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Vickerys_17.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Vickerys_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Vickerys_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_Vickerys_20.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_Vickerys_20.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Vickerys_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Vickerys_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Vickerys_21.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Vickerys_21.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         That evening we had plans to meet Missy downtown at the Cocktail Club to share a party-sized punch bowl before grabbing dinner downstairs at one of Charleston's hottest new restaurants, the Macintosh.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_Macintosh_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_Macintosh_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_MacBar_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_MacBar_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Macintosh_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Macintosh_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Macintosh_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Macintosh_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Sure, a giant punch bowl might sound like a bit much for just three people, but that's why Missy brought her friend Jill . . . and Sue brought
         <em>
          me
         </em>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_Macintosh_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_Macintosh_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         On Sunday nights, the punch bowls at the Cocktail Club are only $20, which is just $5/person for a really good buzz, or $10/person for a really good coma.
        </p>
        <p>
         Of course, you could probably get a punch bowl for $20 in NYC, too.  At a flea market, where it will come with a big crack down the middle and two used Dixie cups.
        </p>
        <p>
         We chose to fill our punch bowl with the Beachcomber No. 2, which contained white rum, brandy, pineapple and lemon juices, cinnamon syrup, ginger beer, nutmeg, and the fantastically named "Velvet Falernum," which sounds like something a natty gentleman might wear but in fact is similar to a low-proof rum infused with lime zest, ginger root, cloves, and almonds.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Macintosh_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Macintosh_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         After recounting our weekend adventures for Missy and Jill, Sue asked if Missy would mind if I stored my luggage at the house the next day while exploring Charleston solo, since Sue planned to depart early to beat some impending bad weather.  Of course, this being the South, not only did both Missy and Jill offer to stow my luggage at their respective houses, but both of them offered me a ride to the airport to boot.  If two strangers in New York City ever make you this same offer, it is very likely that (1) you will never see your luggage again, and (2) no one will ever see
         <em>
          you
         </em>
         again.
        </p>
        <p>
         Soon it was time for our dinner at the Macintosh, where, in a textbook case of
         <a class="external" href="http://mentalfloss.com/article/27992/nominative-determinism-yes-thats-his-real-name" title="This is an external link">
          nominative determinism
         </a>
         , a chef named Jeremiah Bacon is turning out bacon burgers and other divine swine in a chic TriBeCa-meets-Charleston space complete with exposed brick walls, reclaimed floors, and caged pendant lights.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_Macintosh_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_Macintosh_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Macintosh_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Macintosh_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Macintosh_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Macintosh_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The room was too dark for photos, but I did manage a few of the pork shoulder ravioli, which are blurry not because of the dim light, but because your head is likely swimming at the sight of this puffy pocket of porkalicious perfection.  For while pork on its own is good, pork that has been submerged in fat and cooked for eight hours is even better, particularly when whatever has fallen off the bone is stuffed inside a giant ravioli, along with some pork stock and crme fraiche.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Macintosh_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Macintosh_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_MacRav_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_MacRav_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Sue wanted to get an early start on the drive back to Greensboro the next day, so we woke early and made a beeline for one of her old favorites, Page's Okra Grill, a Low Country legend that offers "Local Food for Local Folks."
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Pages_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Pages_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         As well as, "Giant Rocking Chairs for Porch-Deprived New Yorkers."
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_Pages_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_Pages_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_Pages_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_Pages_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         After breakfast, I texted my new friend Jill to find out whether her offer to let me store my luggage at her place still stood, or if that was just the previous night's punch bowl talking.  She responded with the most fantastic text I've ever received from a complete stranger: "I won't be home till 1 but have left a key for you.  Two overly friendly cavalier spaniels will greet you. If you go out, just lock up and put key back in place. Make yourself at home. What time do we need to head to the airport?"
        </p>
        <p>
         I was gobsmacked.
         <em>
          Oh, sure, stranger from New York City who could be an axe-murderer.  Just take my key and let yourself in and make yourself at home.  And if you haven't robbed me blind and kidnapped my dogs by the time I get home, I'll even take you to the airport!
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         And so I dropped my luggage at Jill's house, which turned out to be a manse in the heart of downtown Charleston, complete with two adorable spaniels.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_JillHouse_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_JillHouse_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_JillHouse_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_JillHouse_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         After saying my good-byes and thank-yous to Sue, I had about two hours to kill in Charleston before my flight.  Naturally, I spent them eating.
        </p>
        <p>
         I didn't have a ton of time, so I headed over to Gaulart &amp; Maliclet, a tiny caf also known as "Fast &amp; French."
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_FastFrench_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_FastFrench_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_FastFrench_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_FastFrench_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The space was tight and the seating communal, so it wasn't long before I got to chatting with a lovely woman named Kimberly Glenn, an interior designer whose firm you should definitely patronize because she is warm and friendly and has excellent taste . . . in dining companions.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_FastFrench_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_FastFrench_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_FastFrench_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_FastFrench_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We both ordered the lunch special: French onion soup, cheese and bread, and a glass of house wine.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_FastFrench_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_FastFrench_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Fast &amp; French lived up to its name, leaving me with just enough time to take in some sights before heading back to the airport.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_20.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_20.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_CHSsights_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_CHSsights_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_28.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_28.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_31.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_31.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_30.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_30.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_32.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_32.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_33.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_33.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         One of Charleston's many hidden treasures are the tiny gardens, alleys, and nooks tucked among the city streets.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_21.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_21.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_24.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_24.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_27.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_27.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_26.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_26.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_23.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_23.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_17.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_CHS_CHSsights_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_CHS_CHSsights_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_CHS_CHSsights_25.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_CHS_CHSsights_25.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         As promised, Jill gave me a ride to the airport, and we chatted along the way about the pleasures of meeting strangers and offering hospitality and trusting that your new friend isn't a serial killer.
        </p>
        <p>
         And when I got out of the car, she didn't even drive off before I could grab my luggage.
        </p>
        <p>
         Southern hospitality indeed.
         <br/>
         ------------------------------------------------
        </p>

          <img alt="2015_CHS_ThumbTwo_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/thumb_2015_CHS_ThumbTwo_1.jpg"/>

      <div class="entry">
       <h2 class="entrytitle" id="Entry111">
        <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/111/" rel="bookmark" title="Permanent link to New York, New York: It's a Helluva Town ">
         New York, New York: It's a Helluva Town
        </a>
       </h2>
       <p class="preentrydetails">
        <span class="entrydate">
         03.31.2015
        </span>
       </p>
       <div class="entrycontent">
        <p>
         This month marks twenty-one years that I have lived in New York City -- nearly half my life.   It's quite an accomplishment, really, when you consider that New York is excessively noisy, grossly overcrowded, ridiculously inconvenient, and monstrously expensive.
        </p>
        <p>
         It also happens to be the greatest city in the world.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Arial_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Arial_1.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Arriving home
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         I showed up in a rented U-Haul on a blustery day in March of 1994 to the sound of blaring horns, hollering cabbies, and a cacophony of foreign tongues, all of which I am sure were cursing me out for double-parking on a busy downtown street.  I was overwhelmed and exhilarated and completely unprepared for the unrelenting pace.  Just ordering a sandwich in a deli -- the crowding, the yelling, the line moving at the speed of light and the deli guys all barking "NEXT!" at the exact same time -- was enough to send me fleeing without my food.  Well,
         <em>
          almost
         </em>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         I didn't know a soul.  I had never taken a subway before. I didn't know which neighborhoods were safe, or where to get a decent bagel, or how to negotiate the city's mangled sidewalks in heels.  "Evens go east, odds go west," I'd mumble to myself as I attempted to navigate the bustling canyons.  I didn't dare look up or stop to consult a map, lest all of my NYC nightmares come true at once: I'd tumble into an open manhole, get hit in the head by a falling air conditioner, be mowed down by the passing crowd, and have my purse stolen . . . but not before the thug beat me with it for good measure.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv1_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv1_1.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           My first New York apartment, on 26th Street
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         I was young and brave and stupid all at the same time.  I'd never been jostled by so many people, bombarded by so much noise, or exposed to so many casual and creative uses of the F-word in my entire life.   (Once, in SoHo, I saw a young father carrying his toddler on his shoulders.  When I passed by, I heard him mutter, "Goo-goo, ga-ga . . . what the f*ck does
         <em>
          that
         </em>
         mean?")  Worst of all, I was not at all sure that I'd made the right decision in uprooting my comfortable life in Pennsylvania for one that seemed to promise nothing but hassles.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_PJ_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_PJ_1.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           P.J. Clarke's, on 55th Street
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         In fact, the only thing I
         <em>
          was
         </em>
         sure of . . . is that I was in love.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Food_20.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Food_20.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Rockefeller Center
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_NYC_Anniv_TS_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_NYC_Anniv_TS_1.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Times Square
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Food_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Food_07.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Empire State Building
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_NYC_SoHo_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_NYC_SoHo_1.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           SoHo
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_EVSoHo_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_EVSoHo_2.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           East Village
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_NYCVelvRedo_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_NYCVelvRedo_3.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Central Park
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         And much like love itself, the energy here is a drug (and the only legal one you're likely to encounter):  It draws you in, gets you hooked, and keeps you coming back for more.  Living in this city has changed me in more ways than I can count: I talk faster, walk faster, am faster to offer, er, opinions, and have been exposed to more wealth, poverty, diversity, art, culture, architecture, and amazing food than I ever dreamed.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_chrysler_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_chrysler_1.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Capital Grille in the Chrysler Building
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <em>
          Waaayyyy
         </em>
         more amazing food.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Food_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Food_01.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Coca-cola carnitas at El Camion
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_NYCVelvRedo_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_NYCVelvRedo_2.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Paella at Soccarat
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_BobbyV_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_BobbyV_1.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Cheesesteak at Bobby Van's
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Food_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Food_06.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Skillet sticky-toffee pudding with medjool dates at The Smith
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Buddakan_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Buddakan_1.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Coconut sponge cake with passion fruit pudding at Buddakan
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Annassa_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Annassa_1.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Fish gyro with lobster ragout at Anassa Taverna
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Caf_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Caf_1.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Sparkling blood orange mojitos at Cafeteria
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Food_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Food_14.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Steamed eggs with chvre and sundried cherry tomatoes at Buvette
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Food_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Food_03.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Wild mushroom dumplings with truffle foam at Breeze
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_foodiepics_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_foodiepics_3.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           French onion soup burger at Little Prince
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Becco_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Becco_1.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Cocoa-pumpkin ravioli at Becco
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Food_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Food_17.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Chicken pot pies at Parnell's
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_foodiepics_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_foodiepics_2.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Tilapia with cherry tomatoes and shrimp at La Gioconda
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Food_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Food_18.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Ground chuck and brisket burger at Hillstone
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Food_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Food_12.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Veal parmigiana at Giorgio's of Gramercy
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_32.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_32.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <sup>
          <em>
           The Generous Pour event at Capital Grille
          </em>
         </sup>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_30.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_30.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_31.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_31.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Food_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Food_05.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Birthday dinner at Maloney &amp; Porcelli
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Food_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Food_13.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Birthday milk and cookies at Jane
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_foodiepics_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_foodiepics_1.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Birthday dinner at Le Bernadin
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         Of course, into the life of every food-lover, the occasional crapcake must fall.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Food_23.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Food_23.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         My entire identity as an adult has been shaped by the grit and grind of this city, imbuing me with a sense of determination, confidence, sophistication, and good old-fashioned gumption that I might never have acquired if I'd stayed in Pennsylvania, or moved somewhere like Cleveland or Charlotte.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_NYCVelvRedo_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_NYCVelvRedo_1.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           View from our bedroom
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_10.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           View from our living room
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_03.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           The city's skyline is always changing, and our view now includes the tallest residential tower in the western hemisphere: 104 stories.
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_NYCVelvRedo_7.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_NYCVelvRedo_7.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Our favorite local park, Greenacre Park
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_PJ_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_PJ_2.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Lining up for the Macy's Thanksgiving Day Parade
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_RockCtrTree_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_RockCtrTree_3.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           The famous tree arriving at Rock Center
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_RockCtrTree_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_RockCtrTree_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_RockCtrTree_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_RockCtrTree_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_RockCtrTree1_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_RockCtrTree1_1.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           It's almost ready...
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_NYC-Treelight_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_NYC-Treelight_1.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Crowds gathered for the tree lighting, as seen from Angel's office
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Food_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Food_19.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Cocktails at the Rock Center Rink Bar
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_NYCVelvRedo_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_NYCVelvRedo_4.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Central Park in springtime
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <div class="video">
         <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="281" mozallowfullscreen="" src="http://player.vimeo.com/video/119000822" webkitallowfullscreen="" width="500">
         </iframe>
        </div>
        <p>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Macy's Fourth of July fireworks over the Brooklyn Bridge
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         In fact, New York has turned me into a walking contradiction: I swear like a sailor and argue like a lawyer, but I also know my Prabal Gurung from my Proenza Schouler, and could pick David Chang or Andrew Carmellini out of a lineup.  I speak fluent "restaurant-menu" Italian and have a small vocabulary in both Spanish and Yiddish.  (It's mostly curse words, but whatever.)  I can talk with some authority about the latest exhibit at the Met, or we can debate whether the dirty-water dogs are better at Yankee Stadium or CitiField.  And I completely agree that New York pizza is the best you will ever have (Lombardi's) . . .
         <em>
          and
         </em>
         the worst you will ever have (all variations of the "Original" Ray's).
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_02.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Lombardi's coal-oven pizza
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Misc_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Misc_2.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           SoHo
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_NYCVelvRedo_8.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_NYCVelvRedo_8.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Restaurants along Second Avenue
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         Geographically speaking, New York City is an embarrassment of riches.  Within a two-hour drive in any direction, we can be leaf-peeping in the Adirondacks, lounging on the beach in the Hamptons, sipping wine at a vineyard on the North Fork, relaxing in rocking chair at one of Cape May's Victorian-era "painted ladies," or biking the oceanfront bluffs on Block Island.  Or, you know, watching people pee in the sand in the Rockaways.
        </p>
        <p>
         And if we ever tire of road trips, there's everything from Broadway musicals and world-class museums to dive bars in the East Village and designer boutiques in SoHo.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_SoHo_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_SoHo_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_EVSoHo_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_EVSoHo_5.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           SoHo
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         Oh, and roughly 24,000 restaurants, which means I could eat at a different one every night for the next 65 years, and still never hit them all.  Not for lacking of trying, of course.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_11.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Our summer lunch spot, Dos Caminos
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Food_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Food_11.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Our Friday-night date spot, China Grill
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Food_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Food_08.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           The Saigon-tini at Le Colonial
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Food_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Food_04.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Dinner at Tao
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Food_21.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Food_21.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Food_22.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Food_22.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Our Sunday morning brunch spot, Le Bateau Ivre
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="11018905_1..073550440_n.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/11018905_1..073550440_n.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Our favorite snowy-evening spot, Caf Joul
          </sup>
          <br/>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_17.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           View down our block
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Odeon_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Odeon_1.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           TriBeCa
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         There are so many "only in New York" things to love about this city that it's hard to even name them all, and everyone's list would be different anyway.  Mine would include everything from bodega cats and the Comedy Cellar to chocolate-chip-cookie delivery until 3am and nail salons open 24 hours a day.  It would include the fact that there are nearly 200 bars in the East Village alone, and the fact that you can eat anything here from roasted crickets to ant caviar to goat-eyeball tacos (not that you would.  It was hard enough just typing that).  It would include a local moving company called Schleppers and a Chinese takeout place called Wok to Walk.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_Food_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_Food_10.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Views from my office (with a cameo by my desk lamp)
          </sup>
         </em>
         <br/>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_06.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_NYCVelvRedo_9.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_NYCVelvRedo_9.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Outside my office building
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_25.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_25.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           On my way to work
          </sup>
         </em>
         <br/>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_23.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_23.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_35.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_35.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Views from Angel's office
          </sup>
         </em>
         <br/>
         <img alt="NYC_RockCtrTree2_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_RockCtrTree2_2.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <img alt="NYC_RockCtrTree2_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_RockCtrTree2_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         My list would also include the Manhattan Mini Storage ads for space-challenged New Yorkers.  At least we can laugh at our shared misery.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_MMS_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_MMS_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_MMS_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_MMS_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_MMS_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_MMS_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_MMS_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_MMS_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_MMS1_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_MMS1_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_MMS_6.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_MMS_6.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Also making the list would be the inside-baseball references on
         <em>
          Seinfeld
         </em>
         and
         <em>
          Law and Order
         </em>
         , the Radio City Christmas Spectacular, living within walking distance of Bloomingdale's/Bergdorf's/Bendel, spring in Central Park, sending our laundry out for fluff-and-fold, the bacon burgers at Corner Bistro, and dressing extra-fashionably when I know they're filming on my block.  It would include the free(!) ferry ride to a Staten Island Yankees game on a balmy June evening, as the boat glides by the Statue of Liberty, and even the most jaded among us whip out our camera phones and snap away.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_NYC_Anniv_Food_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_NYC_Anniv_Food_15.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Lower Manhattan
          </sup>
         </em>
         <br/>
         <br/>
         It would include being surrounded by art, culture, fashion, law, publishing, real estate, finance, and all the other industries that make this city pulse with bright, interesting, creative people.
         <em>
          And
         </em>
         people like me and Angel.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="NYC_Anniv_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_Anniv_01.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Sunset from our apartment
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         Indeed, the only downside to living in New York City is that I'm turning into one of those entrenched New Yorkers who won't ever be able to live anywhere else.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_NYC_Anniv_Food_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_NYC_Anniv_Food_02.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <em>
          <sup>
           Park Avenue, midtown
          </sup>
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         Not that I'd ever want to.
        </p>
        <p>
         ------------------------------------------------------
         <br/>
         <a class="enlarge_image" href="/image_enlarge.cfm?src=http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/NYC_SOL_2.jpg" onclick="raw_popup(this);return false" title="Click for full size image">
          <img alt="NYC_SOL_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/thumb_NYC_SOL_2.jpg"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          It's always hard to tear ourselves away from the Big Apple, but this
          <em>
           is
          </em>
          still a travel blog. Up next, time with friends in Charleston, time alone in Paris, and time with tequila in Mexico.
          <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/subscribe/">
           Click here to subscribe
          </a>
          and you'll be the first to know how it's possible for a savvy New Yorker to become trapped in a public restroom on the swankiest street in Paris.
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         Want more NYC?
         <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/63/">
          Click here!
         </a>
        </p>
