      <div class="entry">
       <h2 class="entrytitle" id="Entry108">
        <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/108/" rel="bookmark" title="Permanent link to Xmas in Key West: Come on Vacation, Leave on Probation, Pt 1">
         Xmas in Key West: Come on Vacation, Leave on Probation, Pt 1
        </a>
       </h2>
       <p class="preentrydetails">
        <span class="entrydate">
         03.04.2015
        </span>
       </p>
       <div class="entrycontent">
        <p>
         Of course, we didn't really leave on probation.  But if eating too much, drinking too many, laughing too loudly, and lazing around too often were crimes, I'm pretty sure we'd be sentenced to life without parole after this trip.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_arrest_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_arrest_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         As it was, we compiled a pretty impressive rap sheet during our ten-day spree.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 1: False Advertising
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         On this visit we were joined by our friends Ellen and Brian, who had just started new jobs in
         <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/95/">
          California
         </a>
         when we began making our travel plans.  And so, by the time the four of us coordinated our schedules and decided on the dates for our visit, most of the rental houses we were interested in were already taken.  And it didn't help that we wanted a nightly rental, not a weekly, Saturday to Saturday one, and that the house we originally settled on went to someone else due to a mix-up on the rental agency's part.  And so we picked the best of the bunch from what was left, the Bahama House on Amelia Street.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_23.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_23.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_22.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_22.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_smost_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_smost_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The outdoor space was fantastic.
         <br/>
         <br/>
         <img alt="large_2014_KWXmas_MCBH_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KWXmas_MCBH_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The pool was plenty big enough for four and heated to just-short-of-hot-tub, and was surrounded by comfy loungers, a covered porch with seating for four, and a small gated garden that was perfect for storing our bikes.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <a class="enlarge_image" href="/image_enlarge.cfm?src=http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_06.jpg" onclick="raw_popup(this);return false" title="Click for full size image">
          <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/thumb_2014_KWXmas_MCBH_06.jpg"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_17.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Local_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Local_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The inside, however, was apparently decorated by vampires.  Neither bedroom had a mirror.  Neither bedroom had a dresser.  All of the hurricane shutters were nailed shut, blocking out all the natural light.  And there wasn't a single hook for a bathing suit, wet towel, or black cape in the entire house.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_21.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_21.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         There was nowhere to unpack anything, so we lived out of our suitcases.  We hung our panties from the doorknobs and dangled our bras from the light fixtures.  Within days, there was so much lingerie hanging around that folks thought a new bar had opened in Key West.
        </p>
        <p>
         When we ran out of doorknobs, I fashioned this lovely underwear shelf out of a plastic platter.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We had a washer and dryer, but no laundry detergent, and even if we had, the dryer didn't work for the entire duration of our stay.
        </p>
        <p>
         If the planet runs out of fossil fuels in your lifetime, you can just blame the four of us.  No dryer, plus no hooks for drying (and all shade outside), meant that we went through approximately 400 towels in 10 days, each used exactly once before it was left for the maid so we could get a dry one.
        </p>
        <p>
         Heck, we didn't even have plates.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_cheese_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_cheese_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Okay, I'm kidding about that last one.  But we
         <em>
          did
         </em>
         have only two wine glasses, even though the house sleeps six.  Which, if we're counting down crimes, is probably the worst one on this list.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 2: Petit Larceny
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         Tequila and law-breaking go together like Tracey and tacos, which is why we made not one but two trips to Agave 308 on this visit.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Key West is home to dozens of bars, but you could probably count on just a few fingers those that serve drinks that aren't syrupy-sweet or made from bargain-basement booze.  Agave 308, underneath the Rootop Cafe, is one of those few.  Sure, the dcor consists of sugar skulls and a multicolored marijuana-leaf lamp, but when the food and drinks are this good, you can decorate the place with poison ivy for all I care.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         My favorite drink at Agave is the Paloma de la Fresa, which combines house-made strawberry-infused tequila and muddled strawberries with fresh lime and tart grapefruit to temper the sweetness.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         One Paloma is good, and two Palomas are better.  Three Palomas is just asking to be hauled away in handcuffs.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Angel's favorite, the Mexican Mule, is made with Milagro silver tequila, ginger syrup, fresh lime, ginger beer, and candied ginger, for a hot-sweet treat, served in a traditional Moscow Mule copper mug to keep it perfectly chilled.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Best of all, Agave serves the best pork tacos north of the border, made with house-roasted shredded pork, spicy slaw, and pico de gallo.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Okay, so they might be a little greasy.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         But they're also so delicious that at two for just eight bucks, it almost feels like we're stealing them.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_AgaveTP_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Almost.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 3: Aiding and Abetting
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         To get to Key West, our friends Ellen and Brian drove an hour from San Jose to San Francisco, boarded a red-eye for a 6-hour flight to Miami, changed planes there for yet another flight, then finally landed in Key West nearly 12 hours after they'd left the house the day before.  (That's what you get for moving to a place where going on a hike, not nursing a hangover, is the preferred Saturday-morning sport.)  They arrived at the house dazed and exhausted, plopping down in a travel-weary pile on the sofa for what surely would have been a nice, long nap.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_CM_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_CM_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         If we hadn't dragged them off to brunch, that is.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_CM_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_CM_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         I knew Ellen was still upset about missing the all-you-can-eat-and-drink Christmas Day brunch at the Casa Marina on
         <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/73/">
          our last trip
         </a>
         , and I wasn't going to let her miss it a second time.  And so we splashed them with some tonic water, waved some margarita salts under their noses, and dragged them off to the Casa.  For their own good, of course.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_CM_22.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_CM_22.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_large_2014_MemKW_CM_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_large_2014_MemKW_CM_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The Christmas Day brunch at Casa Marina features carving stations, a mile-long dessert table, and unlimited mimosas that start arriving the minute you sit down.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_CM_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_CM_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_CM_23.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_CM_23.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_CM_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_CM_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_CM_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_CM_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_CM_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_CM_04.jpg"/>

        </p>
        <p>
         The day was glorious, with vibrant blue skies and reggae-tinged versions of our favorite Christmas songs floating on the warm breeze.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_CM_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_CM_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_CM_20.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_CM_20.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_CM_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_CM_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_CM_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_CM_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Of course, even on Christmas Day your teenagers will ignore you in favor of their iPhones, but at least they'll look festive while they're doing it.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_CM_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_CM_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 4: Identity Theft
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         Key West might be a tropical paradise, but you certainly wouldn't know it at Christmas.  Over the holidays, the island disguises itself as a Christmas-y wonderland, complete with Christmas trees, snowmen, Santas, and Abominables.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="KW_Xmas_Velv_30.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/KW_Xmas_Velv_30.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="KW_Xmas_Velv_41.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/KW_Xmas_Velv_41.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="KW_Xmas_Velv_22.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/KW_Xmas_Velv_22.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="KW_Xmas_Velv_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/KW_Xmas_Velv_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Abomin_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Abomin_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="KW_Xmas_Velv_39.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/KW_Xmas_Velv_39.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="KW_Xmas_Velv_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/KW_Xmas_Velv_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="KW_Xmas_Velv_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/KW_Xmas_Velv_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="KW_Xmas_Velv_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/KW_Xmas_Velv_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="KW_Xmas_Velv_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/KW_Xmas_Velv_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>

         <img alt="KW_Xmas_Velv_33.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/KW_Xmas_Velv_33.jpg"/>

        <p>
         Of course, the island can't shed its beachy identity completely for the holidays.  Then again, maybe those are
         <em>
          Jesus
         </em>
         fish?
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_KW_Xmas_VelvFish_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_KW_Xmas_VelvFish_1.jpg"/>
        </p>

        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="KW_Xmas_Velv_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/KW_Xmas_Velv_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="KW_Xmas_Velv_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/KW_Xmas_Velv_09.jpg"/>
        </p>

        <p>
         <img alt="KW_Xmas_Velv_38.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/KW_Xmas_Velv_38.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 5: Reckless Endangerment
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         After a week spent shoveling down everything from tacos and meatballs to pot pies and cheesesteaks, even
         <em>
          I
         </em>
         needed a break.  And so we headed off to Banana Caf for a much-needed green salad.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_TTG_Banana_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_TTG_Banana_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         But this is Key West, where healthy hearts and functioning livers go to die.  And so the salad I so dutifully ordered came topped with . . .  mayonnaise.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         No, I don't mean a mayo-based dressing.  I mean
         <em>
          actual mayonnaise
         </em>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         A few days later I tried again to eat something that wasn't fried in lard, covered in lard, or actually
         <em>
          was
         </em>
         lard. I remembered that Caroline's Caf had a good selection of salads, so off we went again in search of greens.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         I forgot, however, that the best salad at Caroline's comes topped with bacon.  And fried chicken.  And Ranch dressing.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         My taste buds gave me a round of applause.  My arteries gave me the finger.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_20.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_20.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Eventually I just gave up on the salads and had some corn.  Fresh, healthy corn.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Slathered in mayonnaise and cheese.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..nanaCafe_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 6: Arson
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         Is it a crime to set someone's mouth on fire with a toothpick?  If so, then Peppers of Key West would be guilty as charged.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         An emporium of all things hot, spicy, saucy, and sweet, Peppers is the perfect place to mosey up to the bar and get your face melted off.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We started with the milder sauces -- like the fantastic coconut mango, a figgy steak sauce, and a sweet-but-spicy teriyaki -- and then Angel moved on to the ones so hot that they are stored in little coffins and carry warnings about death, diarrhea, and death by diarrhea.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_17.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         You are instructed not to let the toothpick touch your lips, or they will shrivel up and fall off, and to wash your hands before using the restroom, or certain other parts may shrivel up and fall off.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_20.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_20.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_23.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_23.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_22.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_22.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_21.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Peppers_21.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         So far Angel is still intact, but I'm keeping an eye on the situation.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 7: Harassment
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         On every visit to Key West, we stop by Eaton Bikes to harass our friend Chris, who with a patient smile attaches
         <em>
          accoutrements
         </em>
         -- flowers, streamers, and a bell that reads, "Get the %$#@&amp; Out of My Way" -- to my bike, even though he knows that I am a menace on two wheels and that I will spend the next ten days ringing that bell nonstop like a deranged Quasimodo.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Local_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Local_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Local_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Local_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         But how else am I supposed to get around?  Sure, I've crashed my bike into a mailbox (2010), a truck (2011), a curb (2014), and Angel (1999-present), but if that makes me clumsy on two wheels, you should see me on two
         <em>
          feet
         </em>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Local_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Local_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Local_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Local_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Local_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Local_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Local_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Local_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Local_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Local_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Local_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Local_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Local_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Local_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Local_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Local_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Local_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Local_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 8: Bootlegging
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         In the early 1900s, 105 Simonton Street in Key West housed a Coca-Cola bottling facility.  Today, it is home to Key West's first legal rum distillery.  Next time your grandpa goes on about how great everything was back in his day, you can refer him to this shining example of progress.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..stillery_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..stillery_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..stillery_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..stillery_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..stillery_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..stillery_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We decided to do the short guided tour of Key West Legal Rum, during  which our guide,
         <a class="external" href="http://breakingbad.wikia.com/wiki/Mike_Ehrmantraut" title="This is an external link">
          Mike Ehrmantraut
         </a>
         , explained the distilling process and showed us all these cool machines and Angel impatiently tapped his toe waiting for the tasting portion of the program to begin.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..stillery_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..stillery_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..stillery_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..stillery_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..stillery_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..stillery_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..stillery_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..stillery_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..stillery_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..stillery_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..stillery_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..stillery_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..stillery_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..stillery_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..stillery_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..stillery_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..stillery_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..stillery_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Paul Menta, the chef at Amigos Tortilla Bar, is the brains behind this operation, cranking out homemade hootch infused with natural flavors like vanilla brle, key lime, and mojito mint.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..stillery_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..stillery_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..stillery_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..stillery_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..stillery_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..stillery_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..stillery_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..stillery_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..stillery_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..stillery_17.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..stillery_20.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..stillery_20.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..stillery_21.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..stillery_21.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Best of all, next time you crash your bike into a mailbox or feel like eating a bowl of mayonnaise for lunch, you've got a ready-made excuse.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xm..stillery_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xm..stillery_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 9: Fraud
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         About a month before we were scheduled to meet up in Key West, I received a two-word text from Ellen: "Meatball Cruise?" That, of course, is how we refer to the Sunset Sail on the Fury catamaran, which offers crappy margaritas and a decent live band and a great crew and who the hell cares because MEATBALLS!  I naturally said yes and then quickly put together one of those "Christmas Countdown" chains, but instead of counting down to Christmas, I was counting down to MEATBALLS!
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         They didn't have the meatballs.
        </p>
        <p>
         I don't know.  Maybe people complained last time that the meatballs kept rolling off their plates and some skinny blonde girl kept swooping in and scooping them up?  I'm sorry, but the five-second rule applies in international waters, too.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The sunset that evening was spectacular, a fiery orange that faded to a wisp of pink as we made our way back to Key West.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Cruise_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Although we were forced to sail along in meatball-less melancholy, they did have fried chicken, which, even when it comes frozen and is reheated in a Soviet-era microwave rusted out from salt spray, still beats
         <em>
          not
         </em>
         having fried chicken.
        </p>
        <p>
         It does not, however, beat meatballs.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 10:  Criminal Impersonation
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         I am often guilty of judging a restaurant by its nondescript cover, and Deuce's Off-the-Hook is one of them.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Deuces_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Deuces_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Plus, I like booze as much as the next guy, but happy hour at 8 a.m. is a bit much even for me.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Deuces_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Deuces_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Deuces_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Deuces_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Deuces_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Deuces_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Still, when friends Mark and Steven told me that Deuce's was one of their favorite new dining spots, I took a peek at the menu.  And then I jumped on my bike and pedaled over there faster than you can scoop a rogue meatball off a boat deck.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Deuces_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Deuces_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         That's because Deuce's has lobster pot pie sandwiches.  Let's just let that sink in for a moment: Lobster.  Pot pie.  Sandwiches.
        </p>
        <p>
         We started off with the smoked fish dip and an order of spanakopita for the table, followed by the fish sammie for Angel, the gyro with sweet potato tots for Steven, and an entire deep-fried sea creature on a bun for Mark.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Deuces_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Deuces_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Deuces_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Deuces_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Deuces_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Deuces_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Deuces_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Deuces_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Deuces_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Deuces_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         And the Lobster.  Pot pie.  Sandwich. for me.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Deuces_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Deuces_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Okay, so it's not even remotely a sandwich.  But when your lunch entre arrives and it looks like this, are you really going to split hairs?
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Deuces_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Deuces_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         ----------------------------------------------------
         <br/>
         <strong>
          <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/113/">
           Next up, PART 2
          </a>
          !  Hide your kids, hide your wife, hide your
          <em>
           food
          </em>
          .
          <br/>
         </strong>
        </p>
       </div>

      <div class="entry">
       <h2 class="entrytitle" id="Entry113">
        <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/113/" rel="bookmark" title="Permanent link to Xmas in Key West: Come on Vacation, Leave on Probation, Pt 2">
         Xmas in Key West: Come on Vacation, Leave on Probation, Pt 2
        </a>
       </h2>
       <p class="preentrydetails">
        <span class="entrydate">
         03.04.2015
        </span>
       </p>
       <div class="entrycontent">
        <p>
         Our Key West crime spree continues with loitering, breaking and entering, and one cleverly staged home invasion.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 11: Loitering
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         Key West is the world capital of loitering, and one of the best places to do that is at the Southernmost Beach Caf.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_smost_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_smost_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_smost_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_smost_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_smost_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_smost_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_smost_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_smost_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Of course, there's a fine line between "loitering" and "I've had so many frozen drinks I can't get out of my chair."  You know who you are.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_smost_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_smost_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_smost_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_smost_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_smost_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_smost_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_smost_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_smost_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The weather during our visit was hot and mostly sunny, so we also spent a fair amount of time loitering around the pool.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_PoolPics_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_PoolPics_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_PoolPics_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_PoolPics_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="thumb_2014_KW_Xmas_Flippies_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/thumb_2014_KW_Xmas_Flippies_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KWXmas_MCBH_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KWXmas_MCBH_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_treepool_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_treepool_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_PoolPics_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_PoolPics_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         When it wasn't already occupied, that is.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_PoolPics_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_PoolPics_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 12:  Breaking and Entering
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         On Christmas morning, my friend Mark posted the following message on Facebook: "Look what Santa left this morning: Homemade coconut cream pie. Come over and help me eat it."  Didn't he realize that the house we'd rented was less than a block from his own?  I threw on a dress and was barreling through his front door less than 3 minutes later, brandishing my weapons:  A fork in one hand and an insulated to-go bag in the other.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KWXmas_MCBH_24.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KWXmas_MCBH_24.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_25.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_25.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_31.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_31.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         As Mark and I wolfed down the best coconut cream pie I've ever had, Mark's partner Steve decided it would be the perfect time to whip up some homemade macaroni and cheese.  Look, guys: If you want me to move in with you, all you have to do is ask.
        </p>
        <p>
         On top of all this, the pair had just returned from Brussels, and surprised us with a box of decadent Belgian pralines for Christmas.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_26.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_26.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWXmas_MCBH_27.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWXmas_MCBH_27.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         They bring me good chocolate; I bring them battering rams.
         <br/>
         <br/>
         Later that week, Mark made the mistake of telling me that he'd spent three hours making homemade enchiladas for a dinner he'd planned to host for Steve's father and his partner.
        </p>
        <p>
         I think you know what happened next.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KWXmas_MCBH_28.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KWXmas_MCBH_28.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 13: Coercion
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         A few days into our visit, we noticed a pattern developing: Ellen and Brian would walk down to Southernmost Beach Caf, grab lunch, and then spend the day on a couple of loungers at the beach.  But when Ellen developed a blister from all the walking and Brian could recite the lunch menu at Southernmost by heart, we knew it was time for a change.  And so we convinced them to rent bikes and meet us down at Salute on the Beach for lunch.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Salute_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Salute_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         It was something of a disaster.
        </p>
        <p>
         First, it rained.  Have you ever ridden a bike in the rain?   The back tire kicks up muddy rain water.  Raindrops pelt you in the face.  The seat gets uncomfortably slippery.  And you arrive at your destination looking like a drowned rat.  Or, in my case, Bon Jovi circa 1986.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Salute_6.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Salute_6.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Second, the restaurant was packed.  And so we waited, and waited, and waited some more, occupying the time by making mitts out of toilet paper to dry ourselves off.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Salute_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Salute_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Finally, parched and starving and covered in stray bits of wet TP, we were seated.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Salute_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Salute_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         I decided to try the antipasti sandwich, which looked normal to me but, according to Angel, was freakishly huge.  And coming from someone who's lived with me for nearly 20 years, that is not a statement to be taken lightly.  So let's just go ahead and assume that my sandwich looked like one of those ones in the Guinness Book that's 200 feet long and feeds an entire town.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Salute_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Salute_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Salute_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Salute_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Even though my hair, and my belly, had both puffed up to twice their normal size, I agreed to pose with the empty plate.  Angel, and Bon Jovi, would be proud.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Salute_7.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Salute_7.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 14:  Home Invasion
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         The last time we visited our friends Stephanie and Ari in Key West, I fell in love with their sweet little dog, Babka, and may or may not have attempted to kidnap her by folding her up and stuffing her into my handbag.
        </p>
        <p>
         That is, until I saw the newest addition to their family.  Meet Latke, the most adorably ridiculous-looking animal I have ever seen.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Steph_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Steph_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Steph_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Steph_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Steph_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Steph_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         (No, she's not growling; that's just her face.  And yes, that's a mohawk.)
        </p>
        <p>
         As usual, I managed to finagle a dinner invitation by raving about some dish and having someone who actually knows how to cook take pity on me.  When Steph and Ari came to NYC last fall, one of the restaurants they chose is an old favorite mine and Angel's, Osteria Morini.   As soon as I found out they would be there for lunch, I implored Steph and Ari to order my favorite dish, the
         <em>
          sformato
         </em>
         , which is a savory custard made from Parmigiano-Reggiano, butter, and whipping cream, and delivered to Earth on silver platters borne by baby angels.
        </p>
        <p>
         Osteria Morini didn't have the sformato.
        </p>
        <p>
         And if I'd known that ahead of time, it would have been one of the most ingenious plans I'd ever hatched, at least since that time I convinced Angel I had Prader-Willi syndrome and
         <em>
          had
         </em>
         to eat every 30 minutes due to my, er, condition.
        </p>
        <p>
         Because as it turned out, my obsession with the sformato prompted Stephanie to generously offer to make me one on our last night in Key West.  Which explains all those salads on this trip: I was saving up.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Steph_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Steph_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Steph_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Steph_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Steph_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Steph_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Of course, because Stephanie is a Jewish mother (of two canines named for cakes), serving us a ramekin stuffed with 10,000 calories would not do for dinner.  So she also made salad . . .
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Steph_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Steph_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         . . . and the sformato, topped with wild mushrooms sauted in butter . . .
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Steph_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Steph_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         . . . and snapper with pesto, accompanied by grilled vegetables topped with goat cheese . . .
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Steph_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Steph_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         . . . and chocolate souffls with fresh strawberries . . .
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Steph_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Steph_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         . . .
         <em>
          and
         </em>
         homemade coffee ice cream.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Steph_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Steph_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         It was quite a meal, and Stephanie succeeded in making sure that by the end of it, I was way too full to chase her dogs around and stuff them into my purse.  I guess I'm not the
         <em>
          only
         </em>
         one with ingenious plans.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Steph_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Steph_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 15: Conspiracy
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         In criminal law, a conspiracy is an agreement between two or more persons to commit a crime at some time in the future.  If plotting to consume your own body weight in sangria is a crime, then our group dinners fit the bill.
        </p>
        <p>
         Our first outing was to A&amp;B for Christmas dinner, since there is no better way to celebrate the birth of baby Jesus than with cocktails and chocolate cake.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_ABgrp6_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_ABgrp6_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_AB_EB_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_AB_EB_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_AB_EB_9.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_AB_EB_9.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_AB_EB_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_AB_EB_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_AB_EB_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_AB_EB_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_AB_EB_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_AB_EB_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_AB_EB_6.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_AB_EB_6.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         A few days later, we met up with Mark, Steve, Steph, and Ari for dinner at Santiago's.  In advance of our reservation, the six of us spent weeks haggling over what we were going to order and arguing about who was going to go hungry if they had to sit next to me.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Santiagos_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Santiagos_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Santiagos_22.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Santiagos_22.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Santiagos_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Santiagos_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Santiagos_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Santiagos_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Santiagos_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Santiagos_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Santiagos_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Santiagos_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Santiagos_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Santiagos_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Santiagos_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Santiagos_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Santiagos_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Santiagos_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Santiagos_31.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Santiagos_31.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Santiagos_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Santiagos_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         After dinner we stopped by the Orchid Bar.  I may have a tapeworm, but our Key West friends have hollow legs.  And arms.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_OrchPool_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_OrchPool_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Santiagos_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Santiagos_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="thumb_2014_KW_Santiagos_20.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/thumb_2014_KW_Santiagos_20.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Santiagos_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Santiagos_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_Xmas_KW_ari_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_Xmas_KW_ari_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Speaking of crimes . . . this many pairs of dimples in one place really should be illegal.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Santiagos_33.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Santiagos_33.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We returned to Santiago's the very next night with Ellen and Brian for another go-round.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Santiagos_32.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Santiagos_32.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Santiagos_24.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Santiagos_24.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Santiagos_25.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Santiagos_25.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Santiagos_26.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Santiagos_26.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Santiagos_27.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Santiagos_27.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We probably shouldn't have had the flaming cheese two nights in a row, but you know what they say: A cheese a day keeps the doctor . . . on speed-dial.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Santiagos_28.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Santiagos_28.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Santiagos_29.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Santiagos_29.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 16: Disorderly Conduct
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         I attended college at a party school in the late 80s, before the age of AIDS and campus assaults and frowning upon binge drinking.  It was an idyllic time, filled with hookups, hangovers, frat parties, and the occasional bench warrant.
        </p>
        <p>
         And not a day goes by that I don't thank God that there was no such thing as the Internet back then.
         <br/>
         <br/>
         Which is why we never,
         <em>
          ever
         </em>
         bring a camera to the Green Parrot, and especially not when we're pre-gaming with my infamous rum punch.  I'm pretty sure Ellen walked into the pool fully clothed and Brian started licking the walls last time I made a batch, but like I said:
         <em>
          That's
         </em>
         why we don't allow cameras.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_GP_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_GP_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Over the years, I have acted quite the fool at the Green Parrot, egged on by my friend Mount Gay and begged to stop by my friend Angel "My Wife is a Train Wreck" Gonzalez.  I've dirty-danced with men old enough to be my great-grandpa.  I've invited myself to sample strangers' drinks with a two-foot-long super-straw.  I've twirled handlebar moustaches unbidden, and impersonated Mrs. Doubtfire, and belted out my own lyrics to various blues songs at the top of my lungs, none of which rhyme and all of which utilize words that cannot be printed on this blog.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_GP_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_GP_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         By comparison, I was well-behaved on this visit, sucking (my own) beer out of a flamingo straw and decorating my bottle with ornaments "borrowed" from Green Parrot's Christmas tree, which is why I agreed, just this once, to go ahead and snap a few photos.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_GP_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_GP_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_GP_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_GP_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         As soon as I tried to climb inside the popcorn machine, however, all bets were off.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 17: Public Intoxication
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         Friends who live in Key West often lament that there are only two things to do here:  Get drunk, or fry yourself in the sun.  (They're missing the obvious third option: Get drunk
         <em>
          and
         </em>
         fry yourself in the sun.)
        </p>
        <p>
         Not being ones to defy local custom, we spent most afternoons at Louie's, soaking up the sunset and sucking down the pina coladas.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys2_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys2_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys2_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys2_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys2_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys2_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Local_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Local_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Evenings were whiled away at Kelly's, keeping company with their fantastic key lime margaritas.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Kellys_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         In between it was mojitos at lunch, wine at dinner, and the aforementioned rum punch for breakfast.  There's OJ in there, ya know.
         <br/>
         -------------------------------------------
         <br/>
         <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/114/">
          Part 3 is now posted!  Click here to see if we rang in the New Year by commandeering a big red shoe.
         </a>
        </p>
