      <div class="entry">
       <h2 class="entrytitle" id="Entry114">
        <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/114/" rel="bookmark" title="Permanent link to Xmas in Key West: Come on Vacation, Leave on Probation, Pt 3">
         Xmas in Key West: Come on Vacation, Leave on Probation, Pt 3
        </a>
       </h2>
       <p class="preentrydetails">
        <span class="entrydate">
         03.03.2015
        </span>
       </p>
       <div class="entrycontent">
        <p>
         And finally, public lewdness, assault, and some open container violations . . . or, you know, just another Saturday night in Key West.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 18: Public Lewdness
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         You don't really need to go anywhere special in Key West to encounter public lewdness, but it can't hurt.  And so we set off for Better Than Sex, a dessert-only restaurant where you can have a satisfying one-night stand without worrying about how to get rid of the guy in the morning.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_menu2_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_menu2_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_menu_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_menu_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_KW_BTS_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_KW_BTS_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The space is bordello-chic, with lipstick-red walls, dimly-lit crystal chandeliers, and secluded banquettes made for cozying up to your loved one, distracting him with your feminine wiles, and stealing his
         <span style="text-decoration:line-through;display:inline;">
          heart
         </span>
         dessert.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_KW_BTS_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_KW_BTS_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_KW_BTS_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_KW_BTS_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_KW_BTS_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_KW_BTS_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         After perusing the extensive menu, I knew I had to try the Fork-You Fondue, which was described as "liquid vanilla cheesecake fondue."   If those aren't the four sexiest words you've ever heard, then you need to get some new porn.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_KW_BTS_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_KW_BTS_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The others had the "Between My Red Velvet Sheets" cheesecake (which sounds hot but not sexy), the Twist and Stout (which I guess can be sexy if you're into those kind of guys), and the Jungle Fever (which I can assure you is plenty sexy.  Ahem.)
        </p>
        <p>
         <a class="enlarge_image" href="/image_enlarge.cfm?src=http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_KW_BTS_07.jpg" onclick="raw_popup(this);return false" title="Click for full size image">
          <img alt="2015_KW_BTS_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/thumb_2015_KW_BTS_07.jpg"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         <a class="enlarge_image" href="/image_enlarge.cfm?src=http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_KW_BTS_05.jpg" onclick="raw_popup(this);return false" title="Click for full size image">
          <img alt="2015_KW_BTS_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/thumb_2015_KW_BTS_05.jpg"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_KW_BTS_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_KW_BTS_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_KW_BTS_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_KW_BTS_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_KW_BTS_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_KW_BTS_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 19: Assault with a Deadly Weapon
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         Angel and I last visited Latitudes on Sunset Key in 1999, where we rang in the new Millennium with Champagne, fireworks over Key West, and a midnight kiss.  Well, two out of three, anyway.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_oldNYE_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_oldNYE_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         You see, I grew up in Pittsburgh, a city with obsessed with everything from the Stillers and chipped ham to classic rock and mullets.  Lesser-known, however, is the city's obsession with fireworks.  Although most people like fireworks, a 'Burgher will drop everything -- and I mean
         <em>
          everything
         </em>
         -- for some fireworks.  When I was growing up, it was taken for granted that no matter what you were right in the middle of -- driving a car, giving birth, performing brain surgery -- the minute you heard fireworks, the aforementioned task was immediately abandoned because OOH!  LOOK!! FIREWORKS!!!  Thus, a typical telephone conversation might go something like, "So I told that jagoff to kiss my OOH!  LOOK!!  FIREWORKS!!!"
         <em>
          <strong>
           CLICK
          </strong>
         </em>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         And so, as couples everywhere counted down the last seconds of 1999 and prepared to greet the new Millennium, I heard the sound of fireworks down at the beach . . . and promptly jumped out of my seat and ran like a bat out of hell, leaving poor Angel in the dust.  I think he might have kissed a waitress in my absence.
        </p>
        <p>
         Which explains why we haven't returned to Latitudes in 15 years.   But at Ellen and Brian's urging we relented, and hopped aboard
         <em>
          Lil Princess
         </em>
         for the short boat ride over to Sunset Key.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_26.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_26.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_25.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_25.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_29.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_29.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_30.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_30.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_32.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_32.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_31.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_31.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         In the years since our last visit, we'd almost forgotten how lovely the place is.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_22.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_22.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_21.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_21.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_23.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_23.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Soon we were settled in at a table in the sand, drinking in the idyllic surroundings . . . and some mango martinis.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes1_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes1_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         I kicked things off with the rich, creamy lobster bisque, followed by the tuna tartare with sweet chili, soy pearls, seaweed salad, and miso-yuzu aioli.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes_17.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Ellen, Brian, and Angel all ordered the same entre, the cumin and coriander crusted snapper.  This, I noticed, happened at almost every meal -- the three of them ordered the exact same thing, presumably as part of some pact to spread the pain around a bit: I'd beg a few bites from each of them, instead of just commandeering Angel's entire plate.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes1_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Latitudes1_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         But on this night, I was happy to be the odd man out.  That's because we'd just dug into our meals when Angel pulled an inch-long fish bone out of his mouth.  A few minutes later, Ellen did the same.  (Brian claimed not to have found any, but I
         <em>
          did
         </em>
         hear a strange crunching noise coming from his end of the table.)  Within 15 minutes, each of them had enough tiny fish bones lined up on their plate to make a decent-looking fossil.
        </p>
        <p>
         Though we hate to complain, especially on vacation, nobody wanted to get stabbed in the gums with a fish bone, so we mentioned it to our waiter, who summoned the manager, who removed all three entrees from our bill.  It was a generous and gracious thing to do, and as a result we will definitely return.
        </p>
        <p>
         Though Angel is still banned from kissing any more waitresses.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 20: Stalking
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         Our friend Randi is an adorable little blonde lady with a fantastic sense of adventure, a wicked sense of humor, and just enough sense to disable the GPS on her phone when she knows I'm in town.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa2_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa2_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         I guess she wasn't expecting that I'd just stalk her on Facebook.
        </p>
        <p>
         So when I saw that Randi was at La Te Da one fine afternoon enjoying a strawberry-lemon mimosa with fresh basil, I knew what I had to do. I jumped on my bike, mowed down a few mailboxes, and skidded into La Te Da just in time for happy hour.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa2_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa2_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         One mimosa turned into two, which turned into key lime pie martinis with a sidecar.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Which inevitably turned into pizza.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         But as soon as Angel started trying to teach Randi how to change the privacy settings on her phone, I knew it was time to go.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_LaTeDa_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Plus, I'd only had two cocktails and half a pizza, and I didn't want to risk being late for dinner.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 21: Solicitation
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         The vampire cave/house we rented for this trip was conveniently located next door to the Rum Bar, whose cat typically hangs out at the bar there.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_Rumcat_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_Rumcat_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         But because I enjoy having a pet around when I'm on vacay, I naturally decided that the cat should live with
         <em>
          me
         </em>
         while I was in town.  It didn't take long to lure her over.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_Xmas_KW_cat_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_Xmas_KW_cat_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_Xmas_KW_cat_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_Xmas_KW_cat_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_Xmas_KW_cat_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_Xmas_KW_cat_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         And it took even less time for her to make herself right at home.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_Xmas_KW_cat_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_Xmas_KW_cat_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_Xmas_KW_cat_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_Xmas_KW_cat_17.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_Xmas_KW_cat_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_Xmas_KW_cat_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_Xmas_KW_cat_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_Xmas_KW_cat_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Soon she was even making herself useful, chasing chickens off the property for us.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_Xmas_KW_cat_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_Xmas_KW_cat_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_Xmas_KW_cat_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_Xmas_KW_cat_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_Xmas_KW_cat_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_Xmas_KW_cat_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Of course, she wasn't too happy when I wouldn't let her eat the entire bag of treats as a reward.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2015_Xmas_KW_cat_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2015_Xmas_KW_cat_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         By the way, are you wondering how I'm so sure it's a girl?  Because after
         <em>
          I
         </em>
         spent a week feeding her treats, this happened.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2015_Xmas_KW_cat_21.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2015_Xmas_KW_cat_21.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Story of my life.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 22: Escape in the Third Degree
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         Every once in a while, you find a restaurant that's comfortable, comforting, and feels like "your" place.  In Key West, we are lucky enough to have a few such escapes, one of which is Caf Sole.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Then again, it's not hard to feel at home when they are serving bowls of crack masquerading as mushroom soup.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Plus an addictive chickpea spread that I guess is supposed to be spread onto bread, but is more easily spooned directly into your mouth.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         On this evening, as on most others, we ordered our "usual" dishes: the hogfish for Angel, and the shrimp risotto for me.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Xmas_KW_Seven2_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Xmas_KW_Seven2_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_Sole21.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_Sole21.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         For dessert, Angel had the key lime pie. That sounded good to me . . . but not as good as a bowl of gazpacho.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Our other "go-to" restaurant is Seven Fish, a cozy spot with just 40 seats tucked away (at least for now) in a residential neighborhood on Olivia Street.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_17.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         People often complain that Seven Fish is noisy and the tables are too close together, but we're New Yorkers: Half the fun of going out to dinner is eavesdropping on the couple next to us.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_TTGfish_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_TTGfish_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         On this particular night, we started with the wild mushroom quesadilla for Angel, and the Caesar salad with tangy goat cheese and a hunk of Seven Fish's deliciously salty, squishy rosemary focaccia for me.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_20.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_20.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         That was followed by two orders of the coconut-curry snapper over rice.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_21.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_Xmas_KW_Seven_21.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         And just a
         <em>
          tiny
         </em>
         bit more of that fabulous focaccia.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <u>
           Count 23:  Open Container Violations
          </u>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         You might remember that two years ago, we spent New Year's Eve in Key West as hostages,
         <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/75/">
          forced to eat cheesecake and watch strippers and cheer for a lime wedge
         </a>
         .  This year, we were determined to make things more interesting.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <em>
          Way
         </em>
         more interesting.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE2_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE2_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_NYE_tart2_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_NYE_tart2_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE2_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE2_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_21.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_21.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We'd purchased VIP tickets for the shoe drop at Bourbon Street Pub on Duval, which entitled us to an open bar, a buffet of everything from crab cakes and cocktail weenies to key lime tarts decorated with chocolate palm trees . . . and, of course, a bird's-eye view of the craziness on Duval from Bourbon Street's balcony.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_25.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_25.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_NYE_tarts_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_NYE_tarts_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_29.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_29.jpg"/>
        </p>

        </p>
        <p>
         The crowd was filled with folks in wigs, tutus, and all sorts of other get-ups, but
         <em>
          nobody
         </em>
         looked better than the guy with the disco-ball drink holder.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_44.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_44.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_45.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_45.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE2_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE2_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Sushi made her grand entrance about an hour before midnight, signing autographs and posing for photos before climbing into her shoemobile.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <div class="video">
         <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="281" mozallowfullscreen="" src="http://player.vimeo.com/video/121612841" webkitallowfullscreen="" width="500">
         </iframe>
        </div>
        <p>
         Soon it was time for the countdown to midnight.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_33.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_33.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_NYE_EllTra_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_NYE_EllTra_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE2_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE2_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE2_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE2_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We stuck around for a while after midnight, watching a seven-foot-tall drag queen get down with a bunch of male strippers.  Which is a sentence I write all the time.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_40.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_40.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE2_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE2_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_30.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_30.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_31.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_31.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         There was no way I was leaving without getting in that shoe, even if Bourbon Street
         <em>
          hadn't
         </em>
         given us permission.  I figured I'd be long gone before the cops could make it through the mob.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_35.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_35.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_NYE2_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_NYE2_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         But 15 long years later, did Angel finally get his midnight kiss?
        </p>
        <p>
         <em>
          I'll
         </em>
         never tell.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_Xmas_NYE2_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_Xmas_NYE2_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_47.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KW_Xmas_NYE_47.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         ---------------------------------
         <br/>
         Up next, pot pies in New York City, pig parts in Charleston, and pastries aplenty in Paris.
         <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/subscribe/">
          Click here to subscribe
         </a>
         and you'll be notified when a new post goes up!
        </p>
