      <div class="entry">
       <h2 class="entrytitle" id="Entry97">
        <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/97/" rel="bookmark" title="Permanent link to Back to Key West: I'm Sorry I Ate Your Birthday Present">
         Back to Key West: I'm Sorry I Ate Your Birthday Present
        </a>
       </h2>
       <p class="preentrydetails">
        <span class="entrydate">
         12.08.2014
        </span>
       </p>
       <div class="entrycontent">
        <p>
         Of course, I didn't
         <em>
          mean
         </em>
         to eat someone else's birthday present.  Especially since it was intended for a man of the cloth.
        </p>
        <p>
         More precisely, it was intended for the Reverend Gweko W. Phlocker, a delightfully raunchy Key West DJ,  who then proceeded to tell the entire island about my transgression on the radio.
        </p>
        <p>
         But let's start at the beginning.
        </p>
        <p>
         For this trip we stayed in a charming Conch cottage in the Meadows, which satisfied my four main requirements for a vacation rental: Lots of outlets, lots of towels, lots of privacy, and lots of goodies left behind in the fridge.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_CasaBlanca_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_CasaBlanca_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_Redos_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_Redos_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Pool_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Pool_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KWMemDay_Redos_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KWMemDay_Redos_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_CasaBlanca_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_CasaBlanca_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Pool_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Pool_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Pool_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Pool_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BrightLizard.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BrightLizard.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_CasaBlanca_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_CasaBlanca_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We unpacked our things, plugged in the 17 iPads/Pods/Phones we'd brought along, and inventoried the aforementioned fridge, before jumping on our bikes and making a beeline for the Southernmost Beach Caf.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Smost_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Smost_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Smost_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Smost_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KWMem_Smost_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KWMem_Smost_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         There, we had a couple of key lime coladas for lunch.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Smost_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Smost_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Smost_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Smost_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Oh, and sandwiches.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Smost_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Smost_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KWMem_Smost_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KWMem_Smost_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Smost_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Smost_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Smost_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Smost_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KWMem_Smost_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KWMem_Smost_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We spent the rest of the day in a haze of sun, salt water, and wine, which in Key West is called "Tuesday."
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_CasaBlanca_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_CasaBlanca_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_CasaBlanca_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_CasaBlanca_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Pool_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Pool_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Pool_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Pool_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_CasaBlanca_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_CasaBlanca_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KWMem_Pool_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KWMem_Pool_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Pool_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Pool_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         As is so often in the case in Key West, we were joined by a random cat.  We didn't know her name, so we decided to call her Joan Jett. Obviously.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="B5FB808E0C7065F11C7662D78D368D9B.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/B5FB808E0C7065F11C7662D78D368D9B.jpg"/>
         <img alt="JoanJ.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/JoanJ.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_CasaBlanca_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_CasaBlanca_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Soon it was time to get ready for our visit to Big Coppitt.  Yes, I know that name sounds vaguely dirty, and it sounds even dirtier when you consider that it's a derivation of an old English word meaning "thicket."  But our friends Donna and Greg live on Big Coppitt, and you might remember that last time we saw them, they'd been living in a trailer dubbed the Redneck Ranch while they waited for their new home to be built.  The new house was completed last year, but we'd had yet to see it, so Greg kindly drove into Old Town to pick us up, then ferried us back to Big Coppitt to check out the new place and enjoy some wine on the deck for sunset.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Donna_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Donna_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Donna_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Donna_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KWMem_Donna_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KWMem_Donna_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The new house is gorgeous, with spacious rooms, richly stained wood floors, and a fantastic wine cellar.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Donna_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Donna_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Donna_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Donna_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Donna_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Donna_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Donna_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Donna_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_AG_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_AG_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Donna_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Donna_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Donna_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Donna_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         But even that wine cellar had a hard time competing with the view.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Donna_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Donna_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KWMem_Donna_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KWMem_Donna_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         After a few bottles of wine, a lovely assortment of cheeses and crackers, and no small amount of drooling over the size of Donna and Greg's closets, we headed back into Key West for dinner at Square One . . . where they tried to kick us out.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KWMem_SqOne_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KWMem_SqOne_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         But let's start at the beginning.
        </p>
        <p>
         After the short walk over to twinkly Duval Square, we arrived at Square One and were led to a private corner table, which I have noticed is always the case when I am out with one of my girlfriends.  Between the foul language, the reckless imbibing, and the oinks of laughter, we just aren't fit for public consumption.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_SqOne_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_SqOne_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_SqOne_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_SqOne_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_SqOne_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_SqOne_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_SqOne_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_SqOne_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_SqOne_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_SqOne_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We started with a lovely un-oaked Chardonnay, then moved on to goat cheese ravioli, seafood ceviche, a creamy pasta with seafood, and scallops in a rich balsamic drizzle.  I'm not sure what Angel, Donna, and Greg ate.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_SqOne_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_SqOne_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_SqOne_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_SqOne_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KWMem_SqOne_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KWMem_SqOne_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_SqOne_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_SqOne_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We were just enjoying our desserts when the lights went out.  Or, rather, Square One not-so-subtly hinted that it was time for us to go home by cutting the lights.   Later they claimed that someone had turned them off by accident, but I guess they also "accidentally" forgot to turn them back on again.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_SqOne_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_SqOne_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Not fit for public consumption indeed.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_SqOne_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_SqOne_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The next morning we had plans for brunch with our friends Mark and Steven at Hot Tin Roof.   But what was supposed to be a sedate brunch for four ended up turning into the Prosecco version of the Ice Bucket Challenge for eight.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_MemDayKW_HTR_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_MemDayKW_HTR_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         But let's start at the beginning.
        </p>
        <p>
         The Sunday brunch at Hot Tin Roof is one of the best deals on the island, particularly if you like to start drinking before noon and plan to continue straight through to Happy Hour.  Service begins at 11:00 a.m., and then it's all the food you can eat, all the Prosecco you can drink, and all the hangover you can handle until 3pm, a cutoff which has to be strictly enforced since they can't just turn the lights out on you at that hour.
        </p>
        <p>
         I was the first to arrive while Angel secured our bikes, and as the host led me to our table, someone called out, "Oh!  You come into town and you don't even
         <em>
          call
         </em>
         me?"  I wasn't sure if it was my parole officer, that guy whose handlebar mustache I twirled the wrong way at Funk Night at the Green Parrot, or one of the poor souls I doused in Champagne at the Let Them Eat Cake party, but thankfully it was only Stephanie, a woman whose dog I tried to stuff in my purse last time I visited her house.  Whew.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_HTR_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_HTR_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_HTR_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_HTR_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_HTR_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_HTR_17.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         And so, joined by Stephanie's friends Darren and Denis, we pushed the tables together and started calling out orders like a bunch of tipsy auctioneers: "Baaaaaacon-cinnamon-rolls-lobster-mac-and-cheese-key-lime-stuffed-French-toast, do I hear short-rib-hash-and-another-mimosa from the young lady in the blue dress?"
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_HTR_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_HTR_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_HTR_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_HTR_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_HTR_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_HTR_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_MemDayKW_HTR_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_MemDayKW_HTR_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_HTR_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_HTR_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_MemDayKW_HTR_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_MemDayKW_HTR_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_HTR_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_HTR_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_HTR_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_HTR_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         This contraption is a dual salt-and-pepper shaker.  I'm sorry, but asking me to operate anything more complicated than a fork at an unlimited-booze brunch is asking
         <em>
          way
         </em>
         too much . . . and even the fork is really pushing it.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_HTR_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_HTR_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We continued to order food like drunken sailors on leave, the Prosecco continued to flow like water . . . and
         <em>
          then
         </em>
         the tongues came out.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_HTR_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_HTR_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_HTR_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_HTR_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_HTR_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_HTR_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Although no Prosecco ended up being poured over anyone's head, I kind of wished it had.  Because have I mentioned how face-meltingly hot it was during our visit?  Meteorologically speaking, 95 degrees + 100% humidity x 0 breeze = hot enough to have fried that key lime French toast on my forehead.
        </p>
        <p>
         After brunch Mark invited us over to see his orchids, so we made a pit stop back at our house to grab our bathing suits.  Not because we expected to go swimming, mind you, but because at this point we realized that if you're going to sweat through your clothes anyway, you might as well be prepared.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_409_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_409_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_409_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_409_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         And so we showed up at Mark's just in time for . . . more Prosecco.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_409_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_409_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_409_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_409_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Of course, we didn't intend to drink his entire supply.  But when it's 122 degrees outside, it's not like you have much choice.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_409_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_409_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_409_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_409_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_409_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_409_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_MemDayKW_409_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_MemDayKW_409_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The orchids were spectacular.  Then again, New Yorkers are easily impressed with anything that doesn't grow through cracks in the sidewalk.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_409_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_409_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_MemDayKW_409_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_MemDayKW_409_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_409_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_409_17.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_409_20.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_409_20.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_409_21.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_409_21.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_409_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_409_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemKW_409_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemKW_409_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemKW_409_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemKW_409_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The next day, Mark berated me for being a bad influence.  "But we only had three or four bottles of Prosecco at brunch!" I protested.  "Right . . .
         <em>
          plus
         </em>
         the three or four at my house," he reminded me.  Oh, right.  I can't imagine how I forgot about those.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_409_22.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_409_22.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_409_24.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_409_24.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_MemDayKW_409_23.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_MemDayKW_409_23.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         That evening we were feeling a little too, um, forgetful to do much, so we ordered a pizza, floated in the pool for a bit, and then called it a night.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_MemDayKW_Sandy_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_MemDayKW_Sandy_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The next day we awoke early to get in a bike ride before the day got too hot.
        </p>
        <p>
         And by "bike ride" I mean, "raiding the gift shop at the Casa Marina, followed by pina coladas at Louie's Afterdeck."
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_MemKW_CM_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_MemKW_CM_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemKW_CM_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemKW_CM_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_MemKW_CM_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_MemKW_CM_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemKW_CM_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemKW_CM_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Local_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Local_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Local_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Local_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Local_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Local_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Local_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Local_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_MemDayKW_Local_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_MemDayKW_Local_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Later we swung by Old Town Bakery to pick up some sammiches for lunch.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Sammies_9.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Sammies_9.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Sammies_7.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Sammies_7.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Sammies_6.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Sammies_6.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Sammies_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Sammies_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We both decided on the Italian, which came with ham, soppressata, basil pesto, fontina, spinach, tomato, and a prescription for Lipitor.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_MemDayKW_Sammies_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_MemDayKW_Sammies_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Sammies_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Sammies_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Angel once read somewhere that drinking a hot beverage on a hot day can help the body stay cool, so he suggested we stop by Cuban Coffee Queen on the way home.  I'm pretty sure that
         <em>
          I
         </em>
         read somewhere that drinking a hot beverage on a hot day can help the body throw up, so I went for cupcakes instead.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Pool_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Pool_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Pool_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Pool_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Sammies_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Sammies_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KW_CasaBlanca_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KW_CasaBlanca_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         That evening we met up with Mark and his partner, Steven, for dinner at Abbondanza.   Mark hates this place, Steven loves it, and I don't care what either of them thinks because meatballs.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Abbond_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Abbond_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_MemDayKW_Abbond_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_MemDayKW_Abbond_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Abbond_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Abbond_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         My family is of Irish, German, and eastern European descent, but we have always wished that we were Italian, for the food.  And so when I was a kid my father fibbed his way into a membership at the local Italian Social Club, where we'd go for Sunday Gravy most weekends.  The little old Italian grandma who cooked at the Club knew her stuff, including gigantic, tender meatballs just like Abondanza's.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="B3E8299DF7D5B80807E5EE603ACD745D.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/B3E8299DF7D5B80807E5EE603ACD745D.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Are these
         <em>
          polpette
         </em>
         in the same league as, say, Locanda or The Little Owl?  Of course not.  But they are the closest thing I've ever found to that Italian granny's meatballs, and that's good enough for me.
        </p>
        <p>
         <a class="enlarge_image" href="/image_enlarge.cfm?src=http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Abbond_6.jpg" onclick="raw_popup(this);return false" title="Click for full size image">
          <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Abbond_6.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/thumb_2014_MemDayKW_Abbond_6.jpg"/>
         </a>
         <a class="enlarge_image" href="/image_enlarge.cfm?src=http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Abbond_5.jpg" onclick="raw_popup(this);return false" title="Click for full size image">
          <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Abbond_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/thumb_2014_MemDayKW_Abbond_5.jpg"/>
         </a>
         <a class="enlarge_image" href="/image_enlarge.cfm?src=http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Abbond_4.jpg" onclick="raw_popup(this);return false" title="Click for full size image">
          <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Abbond_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/thumb_2014_MemDayKW_Abbond_4.jpg"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         The next day we biked over to Santiago's Bodega for lunch.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_Santi_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_Santi_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_Santi_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_Santi_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Obviously, they understood how hot it was and that one might need to, er, freshen up a bit before entering the restaurant.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_Santi_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_Santi_17.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Santiago's is one of our regular haunts in Key West, so this time around we decided to try a few new items, including the burrata with walnut pesto and the beef short ribs with cherry-hoisin glaze and orange-miso slaw.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KWMemDay_Santi_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KWMemDay_Santi_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_Santi_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_Santi_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_Santi_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_Santi_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_Santi_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_Santi_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_Santi_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_Santi_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_Santi_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_Santi_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Then it was on to some old favorites, like the patatas bravas with aged Gouda, and the croquettes, which are pan-fried potatoes stuffed with ground prosciutto and provolone cheese and served with scallion-studded sour cream.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_Santi_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_Santi_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KWMemDay_Santi_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KWMemDay_Santi_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KWMemDay_Santi_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KWMemDay_Santi_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_Santi_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_Santi_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_Santi_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_Santi_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Later that afternoon we stopped by Louie's again, this time to meet up with some folks from our condo community.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Louies_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Louies_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Louies_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Louies_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The condo contingent had warned us that they might not be able to make it, and after Angel had downed a few of Louie's dark rum mojitos in quick succession while we waited, I was secretly glad they didn't.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="thumb_2014_MemDayKW_Louies_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/thumb_2014_MemDayKW_Louies_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The next day we again set off for an early-morning bike ride to beat the heat.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Lush_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Lush_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Local_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Local_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Local_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Local_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Local_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Local_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Local_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Local_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Soon we found ourselves sitting outside the 8,000 degree kitchen at Sandy's while Angel nursed a 185 degree coffee.  Forget air conditioners and swimming pools for keeping cool, Key West.  What you really need are more coffee shops.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Sandy_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Sandy_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_MemDayKW_Sandy_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_MemDayKW_Sandy_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Later we stopped by Bad Boy Burrito for some takeout.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         I went back and forth between waiting in the shop, where it was approximately 115 degrees, and out on the sidewalk, where it was approximately the inside of a clothes dryer.  No matter where I stood, though, I couldn't help feeling that I was being watched.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_17.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We devoured our burritos in sweaty silence, then spent the rest of the afternoon alternating between floating in the pool, sunning ourselves on the deck, and arguing over a cat.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Pool_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Pool_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Pool_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Pool_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         One of my and Angel's long-running disagreements is what to do about cats that we meet on vacation.  I, of course, am happy to give them free rein of the place.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_CatsRein_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_CatsRein_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_CatsRein_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_CatsRein_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         But Angel steadfastly insists that they remain outside, which often results in a sneaky game of cat and Tracey, in which I repeatedly sneak the cat inside and Angel repeatedly deposits it back outside.   On this trip, however, because the pool area led directly to our bedroom, Angel put his foot down.  Although he claimed to be worried that Joan Jett might get so comfortable that we wouldn't be able to get her to leave when we checked out, I knew that he was
         <em>
          really
         </em>
         worried about finding a single cat hair on one of his shirts.  And so Angel refused to allow her inside at all.
        </p>
        <p>
         Which is how we ended up with one very disgruntled cat outside our door for the next three days.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Pool_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Pool_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Pool_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Pool_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMem_Pool_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMem_Pool_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <em>
          And
         </em>
         one very disgruntled wife.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Sammies_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Sammies_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         On our last day, we headed over to Lush Bar so Mark could show us his new toy: Wine on tap.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_MemDayKW_Lush_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_MemDayKW_Lush_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Despite my pleas, however, he wouldn't let me stick my head under the tap and pour the wine directly into my mouth.  I guess after the Prosecco Incident, he was afraid I'd drain the tap.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Lush_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Lush_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Lush_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Lush_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         In addition to wine-on-demand, Lush Bar offers carefully selected wine and chocolate pairings, beer tastings, coffee and tea, plus dozens of organic and fair-trade chocolate bars.  Get 'em liquored up, then set 'em loose in a room full of sugar.  If this place doesn't need rubber walls, no place does.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Lush_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Lush_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Lush_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Lush_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Lush_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Lush_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_Lush_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_Lush_08.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <br/>
         Mark closed up shop a few minutes early and we popped across the street to the Speakeasy Rum Bar.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         It wasn't long before I dumped both Mark and Angel and cozied up with this cool cat who'd just walked in and sauntered up to the bar.  Not being the jealous type, however, Angel shrugged his shoulders and said, "Canoodle all you want, but you can't take him home."
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The Speakeasy boasts a menu full of yummy rum-based concoctions, including our beloved Painkillers.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         As we sipped and gabbed, Mark suddenly spotted a friend of his.  "Oh!  You have to meet this guy!" he exclaimed, dragging me by the arm to make the introduction.  "Tracey, this is Mozzarella Mike," Mark said.  "Um, actually, it's
         <em>
          Mark
         </em>
         ," his friend replied.  "Whatever," Mark replied to his namesake.  "Listen, Tracey has a tapeworm
         <em>
          and
         </em>
         a blog.  You two should know each other."
        </p>
        <p>
         After some polite chit-chat, I got right to the point: Do you make mozzarella?  If so, where is it?  And more importantly, can I have some?
        </p>
        <p>
         And like a
         <em>
          mootza-rell
         </em>
         magician, Mozzarella Mark pulled a plastic-wrapped log of fresh mozzarella out of his backpack . . . along with a cutting board and an 8-inch butcher knife.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Eyeing this spread, my brain was immediately flooded with questions, to which I received the following responses:  No, he's (miraculously) never been mugged for his backpack full of mozzarella.  No, that knife has never (accidentally) poked through the backpack and stabbed him in the butt.  Yes, I could (thankfully) have some mozzarella.  No, we (happily) don't have to share it with anyone else.
        </p>
        <p>
         And yes, he's (definitely) from Jersey.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         And so we drank and chatted and scarfed down pinwheel after delicious pinwheel of fresh, creamy hand-made mozzarella rolled up with salty prosciutto and peppery arugula, while I thanked my lucky stars, and both Marks, for my good fortune.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_KWMemDay_RumBar_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         When we finally gave up after eating almost three-quarters of the log, Mark distributed the last few bites to the other patrons at the Speakeasy, then started packing up his significantly lighter, but still magical, backpack.  "So, yeah . . ." he began, "I guess I'm gonna have to explain this somehow . . ."
        </p>
        <p>
         Wait, explain what?
        </p>
        <p>
         Oh, just that the log of mozzarella I'd just devoured was actually intended for the aforementioned Reverend Gweko W. Phlocker's birthday, to which Mark had been en route when he (naturally) had to stop for a drink.
        </p>
        <p>
         Reverend Phlocker, I'm sorry about that ugly paperweight you probably ended up with for your birthday.   I'd like to think that if I'd known that mozzarella was supposed to be your birthday gift, I would have restrained myself.
        </p>
        <p>
         But who are we kidding???
         <br/>
         --------------------------------------------------------------
         <br/>
         <img alt="2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MemDayKW_BadBoy_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Want more Key West?  Two more trip reports are on their way, including an 11-day visit over the holidays.
          <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/subscribe/">
           Click here to subscribe
          </a>
          and you'll be the first to know if I manage to eat anyone's Christmas present.
         </strong>
        </p>
       </div>
