      <div class="entry">
       <h2 class="entrytitle" id="Entry95">
        <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/95/" rel="bookmark" title="Permanent link to Northern California: Let's Go on a Friender Bender">
         Northern California: Let's Go on a Friender Bender
        </a>
       </h2>
       <p class="preentrydetails">
        <span class="entrydate">
         06.19.2014
        </span>
       </p>
       <div class="entrycontent">
        <p>
         When our good friends Ellen and Brian moved to northern California last August, we knew that some changes were in store.  Texts and emails and Facebook posts filtered in, painting a picture of their sunny new life spent lounging by the pool and taking long oceanfront drives and eating avocados.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_FinaPalm_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_FinaPalm_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         By January, things had grown so dire that we feared they might start wearing Birkenstocks and meditating.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_EMDapt_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_EMDapt_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         As it turns out, it was way worse than that.
        </p>
        <p>
         They started
         <em>
          hiking
         </em>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         That's right: Two people who were known to jump in a cab rather than walk 10 blocks -- in other words, typical New Yorkers -- suddenly took up that most Californian of pursuits: Hiking.  And they were determined to drag us
         <span style="text-decoration:line-through;display:inline;">
          down
         </span>
         along with them.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2914_EMDTTG_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2914_EMDTTG_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         They'd set for us a jam-packed itinerary of eating, drinking, sightseeing, and hiking (thankfully in that order), encompassing everything from the sea lions in Monterey to the surfer dudes in Santa Cruz to the redwood forest in Big Basin to the tech geeks in Silicon Valley.
        </p>
        <p>
         Our adventure began on a sunny afternoon in San Jose with lunch at Village Bistro in Santana Row, an outdoor shopping area that would be just like one of
         <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/83/">
          the Hamptons
         </a>
         , if everyone in the Hamptons wore hoodies and had invented some app that allows you to take sexy pictures of your cat, or whatever.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_VillageBistro_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_VillageBistro_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_VillageBistro_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_VillageBistro_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         I got a little nervous when our waiter confirmed all my preconceived notions about Silicon Valley by showing up with this nerdy science beaker, but thankfully, it was full of rum punch.  Whew.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_VillageBistro_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_VillageBistro_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_VillageBistro_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_VillageBistro_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Nothing says brunch like rum and fried squid, so we noshed on a huge plate of fried calamari to start, followed by an assortment of salads, seafood, eggs, and, later, a round of mojitos.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_VillageBistro_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_VillageBistro_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_VillageBistro_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_VillageBistro_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_VillageBistro_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_VillageBistro_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_VillageBistro_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_VillageBistro_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_VillageBistro_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_VillageBistro_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_VillageBistro_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_VillageBistro_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         If you've already downed a few rum punches and mojitos for brunch, you'll need something to soak it all up . . . like a pina colada cake.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_VillageBistro_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_VillageBistro_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_VillageBistro_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_VillageBistro_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         After lunch we milled about in the sunshine and peeked into the various shops.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Santana_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Santana_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Santana_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Santana_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Santana_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Santana_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Santana_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Santana_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="thumb_2014_Santana_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/thumb_2014_Santana_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Santana_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Santana_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         You know about these Teslas, right? Only in Silicon Valley would someone show up to a meeting in a $100,000 car and a pair of rubber flip-flops.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Santana_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Santana_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         As Ellen, Brian, and Angel perused the various shops, I mentally prepared a list of all the places I wanted to eat next time we were here.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Santana_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Santana_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Santana_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Santana_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Santana_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Santana_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Santana_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Santana_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Santana_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Santana_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Santana_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Santana_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Back at Ellen and Brian's new apartment, we took in the resort-like setting and marveled at their size of their closets.  (Cat is for scale.)
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_EMDapt_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_EMDapt_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_EMDapt_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_EMDapt_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_EMDapt_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_EMDapt_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_EMDapt_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_EMDapt_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_EMDapt_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_EMDapt_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_EMDapt_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_EMDapt_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_EMDapt_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_EMDapt_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_EMDapt_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_EMDapt_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_EMDapt_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_EMDapt_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_EMDapt_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_EMDapt_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_EMDapt_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_EMDapt_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Ellen and Brian's cats, Peaches and Daisy, are snuggly and sweet, but unfortunately one of them is addicted to kitty porn.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_EMDapt_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_EMDapt_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_EMDapt_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_EMDapt_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         That evening Ellen had made reservations at Palacio in Los Gatos, which is housed in a gorgeous Queen Anne Victorian constructed in 1891.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Palacio_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Palacio_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_Palacio_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_Palacio_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Palacio_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Palacio_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We settled in under the heat lamps on the outdoor patio and ordered a round of margaritas -- the hibiscus for Ellen and Brian, the watermelon for me, and the "caliente," with fresh muddled jalapeno and cucumber, for Angel.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Palacio_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Palacio_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Of course, a similarly-priced margarita in NYC comes in a glass whose size can best be compared to the plastic dosage cup attached to a bottle of cough syrup, so the look on Angel's face is understandable.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Palacio_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Palacio_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The service was a bit slow that evening, so each of us had downed two Big Gulp margaritas by the time the food arrived.  As a result, I'm pretty sure my meal consisted of chips, salsa, enchilada sauce, all of the peas in Angel's paella, and a gallon of tequila.
        </p>
        <p>
         The next morning was The Hike.  Naturally, I prepared by donning white pants, a pair of ballet flats, and a cell phone at the ready to call for a taxi in case my pants got dirty.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_21.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_21.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Ellen wisely planned more of a nature walk than an actual hike, and she picked what is surely one of the most gorgeous parks in California: Big Basin Redwoods State Park, which is home to the largest continuous stand of ancient redwoods south of San Francisco.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_BigBasin_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_BigBasin_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_27.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_27.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_20.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_20.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_31.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_31.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_26.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_26.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_BigBasin_32.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_BigBasin_32.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_22.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_22.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         A sign in the park helpfully provides some perspective on the height of the trees, noting that coast redwoods are roughly 379 feet tall, while the Statue of Liberty comes in at 289 feet and a Tyrannasaurus rex is 15 feet tall.  So next time you see a T-Rex, you'll have some idea of just how tall these trees really are.
        </p>
        <p>
         In addition to really tall trees, Big Basin also has over 80 miles of trails.  And you might think that between two lawyers, one finance guy, and one publishing guy, that we would have enough combined brain power to distinguish left from right.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         But you would be wrong.  And so we were roughly halfway through the 12-mile hike to the beach before we realized that we hadn't seen another human being since we arrived and were probably going the wrong way.  We were a little tired, and a lot hungry, and you know that you are getting loopy when instead of noticing all of the ancient redwoods surrounding us, someone notices a big yellow slug instead.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_23.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_23.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_BigBasin_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_BigBasin_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         And so we retraced our steps, took another look at the directions, and headed for what we thought was the parking lot.  Thankfully we were right, and we stumbled out of the woods exhausted but triumphant, like those people who get stranded in the wilderness and survive on tree sap and bird droppings for a month.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_24.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_24.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_25.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_25.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_BigBasin_30.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_BigBasin_30.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_BigBasin_29.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_BigBasin_29.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We probably should have collected some bird poop just in case, because by the time we dragged ourselves back to the car, it was well past lunchtime and we were famished.  And so we raced back down the mountain toward Santa Cruz for lunch.  Ellen and Brian spent the ride deciding where we should eat and where we should park, while Angel and I spent it deciding which one of them to eat first if the drive took longer than expected.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SantaCruz_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SantaCruz_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SantaCruz_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SantaCruz_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We soon found ourselves at the Crow's Nest, which thankfully had a salad bar.  Angel and Brian stayed at the table to watch our bags, while Ellen and I attacked that salad bar like Gwyneth Paltrow after a juice cleanse.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SantaCruz_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SantaCruz_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SantaCruz_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SantaCruz_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_SantaCruz_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_SantaCruz_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         This fabulous creation is called a Lava Flow, which is a pina colada swirled with strawberry "lava" puree.  I'm not convinced there's actually any booze in it, but whipped cream can make up for a multitude of sins.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SantaCruzNV_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SantaCruzNV_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SantaCruzNV_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SantaCruzNV_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SantaCruz_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SantaCruz_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         I ordered the local petrale sole in a cream sauce with asparagus and little trumpet mushrooms that were so cute I could barely stand to eat them.  Then I remembered that I almost starved to death just an hour ago, so I gobbled up even the teensiest ones with nary a twinge of regret.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_SantaCruzNV_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_SantaCruzNV_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         For his part, Angel went with the Hawaiian poke special, which was blackened and topped with lump crab meat.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SantaCruzNV_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SantaCruzNV_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SantaCruzNV_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SantaCruzNV_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         After lunch we checked out the beach, where those crazy Californians were working out and playing sports instead of lounging in the sun.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SantaCruz_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SantaCruz_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SantaCruz_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SantaCruz_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_SantaCruz_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_SantaCruz_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Then again, it helps to be in good shape around here, just in case.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SantaCruz_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SantaCruz_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         At least there was a bar.  I was starting to worry there for a minute.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_SantaCruz_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_SantaCruz_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         By now it was late afternoon, so we hopped back in the car and took a drive up the Pacific Coast Highway.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="6BEE4F212219AC6817B4B85B12A403B8.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/6BEE4F212219AC6817B4B85B12A403B8.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_6BE7F8882219AC681739D793EAE13F81.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_6BE7F8882219AC681739D793EAE13F81.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The views from the PCH are gorgeous, of course, but the most amazing thing about it is what you
         <em>
          don't
         </em>
         see: McMansions.  The prime real estate along this stretch of coastline -- from Santa Cruz north toward Half Moon Bay and Montara -- is utterly, gloriously pristine, dotted with strawberry fields and pumpkin farms and absolutely nothing else.   And so we stopped here and there to breathe in the salty air and marvel at the untouched beauty of it all.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_6BEA46942219AC6817E9697E7DDCB4B5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_6BEA46942219AC6817E9697E7DDCB4B5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="6BEBA2082219AC68172A123FD6F89ACD.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/6BEBA2082219AC68172A123FD6F89ACD.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="6BED02872219AC681767EFD5CF93CAFC.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/6BED02872219AC681767EFD5CF93CAFC.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="6BE9406D2219AC6817B64B513087886C.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/6BE9406D2219AC6817B64B513087886C.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_6BEFD6952219AC68179EE649A267C5B9.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_6BEFD6952219AC68179EE649A267C5B9.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Our first stop along the PCH was at the Ritz-Carlton at Half Moon Bay, situated on a bluff so breathtaking that it doesn't look real.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_RitzHMB_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_RitzHMB_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_RitzHMB_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_RitzHMB_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Sure, they charged us $10 just to park the car, and cocktails were $18 each, but cozy blankies and fire pits are priceless.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_RitzHMB_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_RitzHMB_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_RitzHMB_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_RitzHMB_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_RitzHMB_6.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_RitzHMB_6.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_TTGFence.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_TTGFence.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_RitzHMB_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_RitzHMB_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Despite having seen the redwood forest, the dramatic cliffs at Half Moon Bay, and, later in our trip, the justly famous beach at Monterey, it perhaps comes as no surprise that Ellen knew a
         <em>
          restaurant
         </em>
         would turn out to be one of the highlights of our trip.  That would be La Costanera, a contemporary Peruvian spot whose name translates to "the waterfront," overlooking the dramatic cliffs and crashing surf at Montara Beach.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_LaCostanera_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_LaCostanera_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_LaCostanera_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_LaCostanera_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Inside, the eclectic dcor holds its own against the natural beauty just outside.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_22.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_22.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_LaCostredo_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_LaCostredo_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Besides the main dining room, La Costanera boasts cozy, fireplace-warmed nooks, a hip downstairs lounge, and an airy dining loft.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_17.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_40.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_40.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_41.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_41.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_LaCostanera_42.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_LaCostanera_42.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_43.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_43.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_44.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_44.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The food here leans toward the light and fresh -- a variety of ceviches, plus shrimp, scallops, calamari, and other seafood -- which was perfect, since we were all still stuffed from lunch.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_20.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_20.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_23.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_23.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         But first we had to get Pisco'd.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_LaCostanera29_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_LaCostanera29_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         A white brandy made from Muscat grapes, pisco originated in Lima, Peru, and therefore features prominently in many of La Costanera's cocktails.  With its hints of apple, grape, and stone fruit, it also plays well with lime, mango, and other tropical juices.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_30.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_30.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_33.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_33.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We kicked things off with the addictive, salty plantain and yucca chips, followed by four bowls of the Kabocha squash soup with shrimp, queso fresco, a hint of pisco, and choclo, which are gigantic Peruvian corn kernels that look disturbingly like really big teeth.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_35.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_35.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Then it was on to an assortment of small plates.  I decided on the snapper ceviche with leche de tigre, or tiger's milk, which is the Peruvian term for the citrus-based marinade that cures the seafood.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_36.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_36.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Angel settled on the calamari stuffed with chorizo and rocoto pepper aioli, while Brian had the tuna ceviche and Ellen went with the tamarind barbecued shrimp.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_38.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_38.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_37.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_37.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         And we all had another round of cocktails, of course.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_31.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_31.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_34.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_34.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_LaCostanera_32.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_LaCostanera_32.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Which was perfect timing for the spectacular sunset that evening.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostredo_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostredo_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_25.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_25.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_26.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_26.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_LaCostanera_28.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_LaCostanera_28.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_27.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_27.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         After dinner, we retired to the outdoor patio.  The air was cool and crisp, the fire pits provided just the right amount of heat, the crashing waves supplied the background music, and the conversation was of the boozy vacation variety ("What the hell am I doing with my life?  Living on the beach in a tent would be GREAT!")
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_46.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_46.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_LaCostanera_45.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_LaCostanera_45.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LaCostanera_47.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LaCostanera_47.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         On Monday morning Angel and I set off for Napa Valley, ostensibly so we wouldn't be underfoot during Ellen and Brian's work week, but in reality so we could geek out at the wineries and gorge ourselves at the restaurants without judgment.  At the end of the week we drove back down to San Jose and met up with Ellen and Brian for dinner, this time at El Jardin, an open-air hotspot in Santana Row.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_ElJredo.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_ElJredo.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LeJardin_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LeJardin_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LeJardin_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LeJardin_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         There, we enjoyed live music, potent margaritas, and the biggest pile of chicken nachos you are likely to see outside of a Chili's.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_LeJBand_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_LeJBand_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LeJardin_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LeJardin_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LeJardin_7.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LeJardin_7.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_LeJardin_8.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_LeJardin_8.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         On our last full day we headed south, to Monterey Bay.  As described in John Steinbeck's book of the same name, the Cannery Row area of Monterey is "the gathered and scattered, tin and iron and rust and splintered wood, chipped pavement and weedy lots and junk heaps, sardine canneries of corrugated iron, honky tonks, restaurants and whore houses, and little crowded groceries, and laboratories and flophouses."
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_CanningCO_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_CanningCO_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MontereyScene_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MontereyScene_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_FishHopper14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_FishHopper14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The honky tonks and flophouses have been replaced by jewelry shops and Starbucks, but the restaurants remain, and one of the best is the Fish Hopper.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_FishHopper15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_FishHopper15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_FishHopper16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_FishHopper16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         They had me at goldfish-bowl-sized cocktails.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_EMD_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_EMD_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Ellen must have pulled some serious strings to get us what was hands-down the best table in the house -- a roomy corner table surrounded by floor-to-ceiling windows on three sides.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_MontereyScene_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_MontereyScene_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_FishHopper02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_FishHopper02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_FishHopper06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_FishHopper06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         After much hemming and hawing over the dozens of cocktails on the Fish Hopper's list, I finally decided on the Monterey Passion, a tropical swirl of coconut rum, passion fruit rum, pineapple vodka, plus banana and melon liqueurs.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_FishHopper05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_FishHopper05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         As usual, however, Ellen won the Best Drink Derby by a mile, literally flaming the competition.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_FishHopper03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_FishHopper03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Lunch began with the Fish Hopper's famous clam chowder, which has been voted Best Clam Chowder in Monterey County nine years in a row.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_FishHopper17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_FishHopper17.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_FishHopper18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_FishHopper18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The only thing that could have made that chowder any better is serving it with a side of $100 bills.
        </p>
        <p>
         That was followed by three orders of the macadamia-nut-crusted halibut with caramelized sweet potatoes for Ellen, Brian, and Angel, and the crab-and-shrimp stuff petrale sole with fava beans, mushrooms, artichokes, spinach, and a light saffron broth for me.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_FishHopper07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_FishHopper07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_FishHopper19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_FishHopper19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The clam chowder was small, and the fish was light, which is all I can think of to justify what happened next.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_FishHopper09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_FishHopper09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_FishHopper10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_FishHopper10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_FishHopper08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_FishHopper08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The irony is not lost on me that, after stuffing ourselves silly at lunch, we headed over to the pier to see the sea lions, an animal whose favorite pastime is flopping about on its giant belly.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_MontereyScene_20.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_MontereyScene_20.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The day was extraordinarily windy, which is always a problem for me because of my eyes, which Angel refers to as The Vortex.  My eyes are big, and my eyelashes are freakishly long -- so long that I actually trimmed them once in junior high because they kept hitting the insides of my sunglasses.  (You can just leave your hate mail in the comments.)  Combined, they attract all manner of dirt, dust, and other assorted items (I have actually bitten into a potato chip and had the shrapnel end up in my eye).  And so, "Wait, there's something in my eye" is the only phrase that I utter with more frequency than "Are you gonna eat that?"
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_MontereyScene_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_MontereyScene_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Which explains why I tried to pry the helmet off this sculpture and attach it to my own head.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MontereyScene_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MontereyScene_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         In the end it was a good thing I couldn't get it off, or I might have missed the spectacular scenery all around us.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_MontereyScene_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_MontereyScene_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MontereyScene_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MontereyScene_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MontereyScene_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MontereyScene_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_MontereyScene_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_MontereyScene_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>

        </p>
        <p>
         In addition to the area's natural beauty, Monterey is full of quaint shops, small cafes, and manicured oceanfront parks.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MontereyScene_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MontereyScene_02.jpg"/>
        </p>

        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_MontereyScene_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_MontereyScene_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_MontereyScene_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_MontereyScene_04.jpg"/>

        </p>
        <p>
         Sometimes the best laid plans are no plans at all, and on our way to the pier we were thrilled to stumble upon the annual Monterey Rock &amp; Rod Festival, featuring hundreds of classic cars and an old-fashioned sock hop.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_CarShow_49.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_CarShow_49.jpg"/>

         The four of us nearly gave ourselves whiplash trying take in all the fins and fuzzy dice, while the band played "Trac(e)y" by The Cufflinks.

        <p>
         <img alt="2014_CarShow_25.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_CarShow_25.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         And just when I thought things couldn't get any better, one of the car's owners approached me and asked if I'd like to sit in the car and have my photo taken. While wearing a FABULOUS FAUX FUR.   Is that even a question?  Not even bothering to open the door, I hopped through the open window Dukes of Hazzard-style, flung my new fur over my shoulders, urged Ellen to jump into the passenger seat, and savored every minute of our "Thelma and Louise" re-enactment.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_CarShow_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_CarShow_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_CarShow_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_CarShow_09.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <br/>
         We couldn't believe our luck when a second car owner invited us to sit inside, this time in a bubblegum pink confection called the Pink Lady.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_CarShow_24.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_CarShow_24.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_CarShow_23.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_CarShow_23.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         As Angel posed in the driver's seat, the owner asked me, "Is that your husband?"  When I answered yes, she good-naturedly elbowed me in the ribs and said saucily, "
         <em>
          Luckyyy
         </em>
         !  Look at that smile!"  Yes, he's very cute.  When he isn't making fun of The Vortex or refusing to give me half his dinner.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_CarShow_26.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_CarShow_26.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We made our final rounds, delighting in the shiny fenders, gleaming fins, and funky hood ornaments.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_CarShow_46.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_CarShow_46.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_CarShow_43.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_CarShow_43.jpg"/>

        <p>
         <img alt="2014_CarShow_47.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_CarShow_47.jpg"/>

        <p>
         <img alt="2014_CarShow_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_CarShow_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Although the car show had been great, our reason for visiting Monterey had been to see the sea lions, and so we headed back over towards the water. . .very carefully.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SeaLions_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SeaLions_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SeaLions_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SeaLions_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SeaLions_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SeaLions_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         As we walked along Ellen looked in all their usual haunts, and right when I started to worry that they'd all gone home for the day, we heard the unmistakable honk of the sea lion, which can best be described as a cross between an irate duck, my sinuses on a bad day, and a kazoo.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_SeaLions_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_SeaLions_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Besides the sound, we were also completely unprepared for how playful they are.  Like slippery, overgrown puppies, the sea lions chased each other around, performed back flips and side floats, and flopped onto their backs -- and over each other -- to bask in the sunshine.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_SeaLionRedos_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_SeaLionRedos_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_SeaLions_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_SeaLions_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_Sealions1_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_Sealions1_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SeaLions_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SeaLions_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_Sealions_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_Sealions_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Sealions_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Sealions_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         I could have watched the sea lions frolicking all day, but more sights beckoned, and so we took a quick trip down the pier to check out the shops, as well as the restaurants' free samples of clam chowder.  Sure, I was already stuffed from lunch, but
         <em>
          somebody
         </em>
         had to make sure the Fish Hopper's chowder really deserved all those awards.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SeaLionRedos_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SeaLionRedos_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SeaLions_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SeaLions_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SeaLions_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SeaLions_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SeaLions_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SeaLions_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SeaLions_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SeaLions_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SeaLions_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SeaLions_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         As we strolled along, we spotted this animal trying to swallow a Chihuahua whole.   Is it a giant wolf-dog?  A small, mangy horse?  Let's just compromise and call it a Dorse.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_SeaLions_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_SeaLions_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Soon it was time to head back to San Jose.  We had dinner reservations for that evening at a restaurant in nearby Saratoga, but the day had been so filled with fun and sun and wind that none of us were feeling up to changing for dinner by the time we made it back home.
        </p>
        <p>
         So we decided to get kinky in the hot tub instead.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_InNOut_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_InNOut_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Get your mind out of the gutter, would you?  I'm just talking about booze . . . again.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_InNOut_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_InNOut_17.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         In fact, we were so exhausted that I had just enough time to eat half of a large pepperoni pizza and cozy up on the couch for the first half-hour of "Jurassic Park" before I completely passed out.  (As Brian lamented the next day, "You didn't even get to see anyone get eaten!")
        </p>
        <p>
         Our flight was scheduled to leave the next afternoon, so we had time for one more meal before heading home.   And because she is a good and true friend, Ellen agreed to forego a normal brunch and take me here instead:
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_InNOut_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_InNOut_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_InNOut_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_InNOut_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_InNOut_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_InNOut_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         You didn't really expect me to leave Cali without trying one, or four, did you?
        </p>
        <p>

        <p>
         One burger tasted like a second one, so Angel went back up to the counter to order us another round.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_InNOut_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_InNOut_03.jpg"/>
        </p>

         <img alt="large_2014_BurgerRedoINO_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_BurgerRedoINO_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Sure, two burgers and a mound of fries aren't the healthiest of breakfasts, but now I get it:
         <em>
          That's
         </em>
         what hiking is for.
         <br/>
         ------------------------------------------------------------------
         <br/>
         Next up,
         <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/96/">
          a wine-soaked trip to the Napa Valley
         </a>
         , a rum-soaked trip to Key West, and another sweat-soaked summer in the Hamptons!
        </p>
       </div>

      <div class="entry">
       <h2 class="entrytitle" id="Entry83">
        <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/83/" rel="bookmark" title="Permanent link to Tiptoe Through the Hedgerow: The Hamptons From A to Z ">
         Tiptoe Through the Hedgerow: The Hamptons From A to Z
        </a>
       </h2>
       <p class="preentrydetails">
        <span class="entrydate">
         04.14.2014
        </span>
       </p>
       <div class="entrycontent">
        <p>
         It's spring!  That time of year when we move our clocks forward, clean our houses for the first time since Halloween, and drag an unsuspecting groundhog out of his hidey-hole to tell us whether we should bury our winter coats in the back of the closet, or just bury ourselves under the covers.  And for me, it's also that time of year when I start getting giddy at the thought of spending weekends at our cottage in the Hamptons.
        </p>
        <p>
         Sure, the Hamptons are overpriced, overcrowded, and often filled with what I'd hoped to leave behind in New York City . . . but those are only
         <em>
          some
         </em>
         of the reasons why I love it.  Here are 26 others.
        </p>
        <h3>
         A is for Almond.
        </h3>
        <p>
         A classic French bistro with a great wine list and fantastic food, Almond is the kind of place where you can snuggle in with some steak frites and a glass of Bordeaux in the winter, or enjoy the breeze from the flung-open French doors and a fig martini at the bar in the summer.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_Almond_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_Almond_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Almondretry.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/Almondretry.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_AlmondBar_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_AlmondBar_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_Almond_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_Almond_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         A is also for Alan Alda, who also dines at Almond, and to whom I once sent a fan letter.  (I watched a lot of M*A*S*H after school.  It came in great with the rabbit ears on our TV.)  After surreptitiously snapping this photo of him at Almond a few summers ago, I was
         <em>
          thisclose
         </em>
         to interrupting his dinner to ask, "Hey, do you remember that fan letter you got from that 8-year-old girl that time?"
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_Almond_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_Almond_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         You know he does.  Nobody could forget something
         <em>
          that
         </em>
         weird.
        </p>
        <h3>
         B is for Beacon.
        </h3>
        <p>
         Located atop a fancy yacht club in Sag Harbor, Beacon boasts excellent food, friendly service, and a postcard view, which is why you will find us here almost every weekend.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_Beacon_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_Beacon_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_Beacon_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_Beacon_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_Beacon_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_Beacon_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_Beacon_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_Beacon_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Of course, we had to tell our accountant that we're broke due to huge gambling losses, but it still sounds better than, "I'm paying the mortgage over at Beacon."
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_Beacon_6.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_Beacon_6.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_Beacon_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_Beacon_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Beacon_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Beacon_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <h3>
         C is for Cowfish.
        </h3>
        <p>
         The Hamptons are all about the water views, and one of the best can happily be found within a 10-minute drive of our cottage.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_Cowfish_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_Cowfish_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_Cowfish_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_Cowfish_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Cowfish, however, ups the ante with its location on a small peninsula, affording water views on
         <em>
          three
         </em>
         sides, thus avoiding the temper tantrums that can occur when a Hamptonite suspects that he didn't get the best table in the house.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_Cowfish_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_Cowfish_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_Cowfish_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_Cowfish_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_Cowfish_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_Cowfish_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_Cowfish_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_Cowfish_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_Cowfish_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_Cowfish_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_Cowfish_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_Cowfish_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         And with an outdoor bar/living room, house-made rum punch served in chilled Mason jars, and the freshest seafood around, it's easy to understand why we're on first-name basis with the waitstaff and the owner named his first kid Trangel.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_Cowfish_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_Cowfish_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_Cowfish_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_Cowfish_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_Cowfish_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_Cowfish_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_Cowfish_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_Cowfish_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_Cowfish_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_Cowfish_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <h3>
         D is for Dockers.
        </h3>
        <p>
         Fourteen years ago, Dockers was a casual little spot on the bay that served as the post-party after our wedding.  It's where we danced on the tables and the DJ played the chicken dance and one of my girlfriends threw up in the bushes.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Hamptons_Dockers_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/Hamptons_Dockers_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Hamptons_Dockers_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/Hamptons_Dockers_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Hamptons_Dockers_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/Hamptons_Dockers_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Hamptons_Dockers_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/Hamptons_Dockers_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_dockersboat2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_dockersboat2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Today, Dockers is done up in crisp navy-and-white fabric and oversized hurricane lamps, and the drinks are way too expensive to get all that drunk, but the friendly service and stunning sunsets haven't changed one bit.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_Hamptons_Dockers_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_Hamptons_Dockers_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Hamptons_Dockers_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/Hamptons_Dockers_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Hamptons_Dockers_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/Hamptons_Dockers_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_Hamptons_Dockers_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_Hamptons_Dockers_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Hamptons_Dockers_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/Hamptons_Dockers_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_Hamptons_Dockers_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_Hamptons_Dockers_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <h3>
         E is for East Hampton.
        </h3>
        <p>
         In 1725, Dick Syme was elected Common Whipper for East Hampton and was paid 3 shillings for each person whipped.  Of course, there is no Common Whipper in East Hampton today; instead, the town extracts its pound of flesh by charging $700 a night for a hotel room and $40 for a bowl of pasta.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="EH-Velvia3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/EH-Velvia3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="EH-Velvia8.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/EH-Velvia8.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="EH-Velvia5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/EH-Velvia5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="EH_okay_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/EH_okay_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         You didn't think National Geographic's "Most Beautiful Village in America" was going to come cheap, did you?
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_EHover_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_EHover_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_huntting.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_huntting.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_EHover_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_EHover_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_EHover_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_EHover_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_EH_okay_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_EH_okay_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <h3>
         F is for fall.
        </h3>
        <p>
         Though it's hard to top a sultry August afternoon in the Hamptons, fall is even more sublime.  The crowds have migrated back to the city, the ocean is still warm, it's harvest time at the vineyards, and restaurant menus are bursting with locally-grown apples, pumpkins, chestnuts, and Brussels sprouts.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_EQFall_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_EQFall_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_EQFall_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_EQFall_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_EQFall_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_EQFall_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_EQFall_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_EQFall_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_EQFall_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_EQFall_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_EQFall_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_EQFall_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_EQFall_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_EQFall_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_EQFall_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_EQFall_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_EQFall_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_EQFall_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_EQFall_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_EQFall_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_EQFall_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_EQFall_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Best of all, there's trick-or-treating in the villages, and Angel and I are easily mistaken for oversized hobos, which results in a pretty nice haul.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_VelviaTorT.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_VelviaTorT.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <h3>
         G is for the Greenport Brewing Company.
        </h3>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_Greenport4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_Greenport4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Ros is all the rage in the Hamptons, but at least once a season Angel shrugs off his pastel polo, ditches the Brooks Brothers khakis, tucks in his pinky finger, and guzzles some beer.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_Greenport6.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_Greenport6.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         I go along for the great shopping in Greenport, since the best way to pry your husband's fingers off his credit card is to wrap them around a pint glass.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Husbandbench_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Husbandbench_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="calypso.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/calypso.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <h3>
         H is for house drinks.
        </h3>
        <p>
         It seems that every bar and restaurant in the Hamptons has a "specialty" cocktail, and picking a favorite is like picking your favorite kid:  It can be done, but not without some hurt feelings.  That's why I have several favorites.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="HouseDrinks_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/HouseDrinks_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Besides being a boozy summer picnic in a glass, the watermelon margarita at B. Smith's in Sag Harbor tastes a bit different every year depending on the quality of that summer's watermelon crop.  And so we find ourselves obsessively consulting our Farmer's Almanac and saying things like, "Ah, yes, the summer of '96.  Now
         <em>
          that
         </em>
         was a great year."
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_zzz_9.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_zzz_9.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The Prickly Pear at Rumba in Hampton Bays is both sweet and tart, and the color is even more delicious.  But do not be fooled: Two of these babies and you will be pronouncing them "Plucky Purrs."
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Rumba_Prickly_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Rumba_Prickly_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The blueberry mojito at Docker's may come in a small glass, but it's chock-full of memories, from wild weekends with my sister to romantic sunsets with Angel to leisurely Sunday brunches in early spring when the sun finally begins to warm our backs.  Over the years the price has increased dramatically, but can you really put a price on happiness?
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="HouseDrinks_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/HouseDrinks_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Apparently you can, and that price is roughly $8 an ounce.
        </p>
        <p>
         And then there's the Sweet Life, an off-the-menu special at Rumba, which I think is my
         <em>
          favorite
         </em>
         favorite.  Maybe it's because it tastes exactly like the homemade limeade my mom used to make to take along on summer picnics . . . which I now realize must have been spiked with gin.  Mama was no dummy.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_HouseDrinks_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_HouseDrinks_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <h3>
         I is for Italian food.
        </h3>
        <p>
         Long Island's climate is similar to that of Naples, Italy (they share the same latitude), and therefore many of the best things about Italian food -- tomatoes, basil, asparagus, spinach, squash, and melons -- grow like gangbusters on Long Island, to say nothing of the fresh seafood and abundance of dairy farms.  And no place puts those ingredients to better use than Tutto Il Giorno, an intimate spot off the beaten path on Nugent Street in Southampton.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Tutto_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Tutto_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Tutto_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Tutto_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Tutto_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Tutto_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Tutto_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Tutto_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Tutto_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Tutto_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Yes, the portions will be on the small side, and the bill will rival the GDP of a small island, but if the Lear is in the shop and you can't make it to Italy for the weekend, Tutto is a pretty good substitute.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Tutto_6.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Tutto_6.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Tutto_8.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Tutto_8.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_Tutto_7.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_Tutto_7.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <h3>
         J is for John Scott's Surf Shack.
        </h3>
        <p>
         An open-air surf shack tucked among the million-dollar homes along Dune Road in Westhampton Beach, John Scott's is the perfect place to kick back Hamptons-style, with a cold beer, a bucket of popcorn shrimp, and the knowledge that Anderson Cooper lives just down the street.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_JohnScotts_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_JohnScotts_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_JohnScotts_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_JohnScotts_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_JohnScotts_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_JohnScotts_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_JohnScotts_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_JohnScotts_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <h3>
         K is for killer views.
        </h3>
        <p>
         At least there's
         <em>
          something
         </em>
         to do while you're sitting in traffic.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_Views_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_Views_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Views_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Views_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_killerview2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_killerview2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Views_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Views_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2014_Views_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2014_Views_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2014_Views_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2014_Views_09.jpg"/>

         <img alt="large_vineyard2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_vineyard2.jpg"/>
