      <div class="entry">
       <h2 class="entrytitle" id="Entry90">
        <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/90/" rel="bookmark" title="Permanent link to The BVIs, Part 2: We're Just a Couple of Swingers">
         The BVIs, Part 2: We're Just a Couple of Swingers
        </a>
       </h2>
       <p class="preentrydetails">
        <span class="entrydate">
         01.30.2014
        </span>
       </p>
       <div class="entrycontent">
        <p>
         Back on Virgin Gorda, during a day trip in which we locked ourselves out of our car, defied the AARP by climbing a bunch of ladders at the Baths, ended up on a blacklist for latecomers at Little Dix Bay, and then proceeded to eat their restaurant out of all its pepperoni, potato chips, and rum, we were now in something of a food coma.  And so our waitress suggested that we take a look around the property and told us to feel free to relax on the beach loungers or take a swim.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixLunchRedo_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixLunchRedo_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         That was our first inkling that Little Dix is truly someplace special.  Not only is the service impeccable, but the staff there truly cares, and the pride that showed on the faces of everyone we encountered -- from the gardeners to the waitstaff to the shuttle drivers -- was lovely to see, particularly in a part of the world that often gets a bad rap for service.  "Have you seen the main dining room?" they asked, beaming.  "What about the pool?"  "Oh, but you must visit our spa before you leave!" they urged us, their eyes lighting up.  It wasn't a sales pitch.  It wasn't formal, forced politeness.  It was a warm, welcoming embrace, and we quickly realized that Little Dix treated a couple of day-tripping interlopers better than some of the high-end resorts we've actually
         <em>
          stayed
         </em>
         at.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixLunch_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixLunch_10.jpg"/>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixLunch_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixLunch_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_DixLunch_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_DixLunch_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         And so we checked out the beach and the grounds . . .
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixGen_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixGen_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixGen_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixGen_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixGen_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixGen_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixGen_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixGen_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixGen_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixGen_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixGen_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixGen_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixGen_20.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixGen_20.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixGen_21.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixGen_21.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixGen_22.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixGen_22.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixGen_23.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixGen_23.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixGen_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixGen_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         and the main dining room . . .
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixGen_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixGen_17.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixGen_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixGen_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixGen_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixGen_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixGen_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixGen_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixGen_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixGen_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         and the pool . . .
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_DixGen_24.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_DixGen_24.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_DixGen_26.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_DixGen_26.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixGen_27.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixGen_27.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         . . . and, to AmEx's great delight, the well-stocked gift shop.
        </p>
        <p>
         Later, we hopped in one of the complimentary golf cart shuttles that roam the resort -- the main stop for which is at "deh big tree" -- and climbed the hill up to Sense, the spa at Little Dix that we'd heard so much about.  There, we were greeted with our choice of lemon or orange water and given free reign to explore at our leisure.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixGen_28.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixGen_28.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixPoolRedo_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixPoolRedo_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_DixSpa_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_DixSpa_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixSpa_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixSpa_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixSpa_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixSpa_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixSpa_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixSpa_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         If you actually climb the dozens of near-vertical steps up to this platform, yoga itself would seem to be overkill.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixSpa_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixSpa_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixSpa_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixSpa_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Besides, you will be too busy taking in the incredible view to worry about perfecting your downward dog.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixSpa_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixSpa_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_DixSpa_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_DixSpa_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixSpa_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixSpa_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_DixSpa_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_DixSpa_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixSpa_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixSpa_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Once we descended from the yoga platform, we made our way past the infinity pool to a steep stone path that leads to a secluded, secret beach.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixSpa_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixSpa_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixSpa_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixSpa_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_DixSpa_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_DixSpa_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Obviously we had no choice but to act out the surf scene in "From Here to Eternity" here.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixSpa_20.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixSpa_20.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixSpa_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixSpa_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixSpa_21.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixSpa_21.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DixSpa_22.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DixSpa_22.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         It was no small task to pry ourselves away from the beauty of Little Dix, particularly since we were adapting quite nicely to being treated like visiting royalty, but eventually we made our way over to Coco Maya, a chic new spot on the beach known for its sleek decor and sexy cocktails.
        </p>
        <p>
         Coco Maya was like a big, beachy showroom for all my favorite things: Edison bulbs, fire pits, cushy couches, ivy walls, beds-for-two on the beach, and booze.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CocoMaya_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CocoMaya_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CocoMaya_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CocoMaya_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CocoMaya_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CocoMaya_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CocoMaya_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CocoMaya_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CocoMaya_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CocoMaya_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_CocoMaya_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_CocoMaya_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CocoMaya_19.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CocoMaya_19.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CocoMaya_20.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CocoMaya_20.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         And just when I thought that I couldn't be any more in love with this place, I saw
         <em>
          this
         </em>
         at the end of the bar.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CocoMaya_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CocoMaya_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Oh, how I loved that swing.  I loved it the way I love the corner booth in a cozy bistro, or the window seat on an airplane, or any seat on the subway.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CocoMaya_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CocoMaya_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_CocoMaya_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_CocoMaya_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         That day's special was a mango daiquiri, which was made simply and from scratch, with freshly cubed mangoes, rum, and a pinch of sugar, as opposed to the cloying, sugary syrup that so many other daiquiris are made from.  For his part, Angel went with the Passion Martini, which was made with pured passion fruit, raspberry vodka, guava, and a bit of chili, this last ingredient both adding some kick and ensuring that Angel got a drink all to himself for once.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_chili_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_chili_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CocoMaya_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CocoMaya_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CocoMaya_21.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CocoMaya_21.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CocoMaya_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CocoMaya_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_CocoMaya_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_CocoMaya_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Don't have too many cocktails, though, or you might get confused about which bathroom to use.
        </p>
        <p>
         <a class="enlarge_image" href="/image_enlarge.cfm?src=http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CocoMaya_23.jpg" onclick="raw_popup(this);return false" title="Click for full size image">
          <img alt="2013_BVI_CocoMaya_23.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/thumb_2013_BVI_CocoMaya_23.jpg"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         Out back, Coco Maya has a cool "game room," with more couches and a couple of dart boards nestled among the boulders.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CocoMaya_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CocoMaya_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CocoMaya_17.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CocoMaya_17.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         There was a small playground, too, because we all know how well children mix with alcohol and flying darts.
        </p>
        <p>
         The day's forecast had called for an 80% chance of rain, and sure enough, by late afternoon, the clouds began to roll in in earnest.  As we swung and sipped, the sky darkened to a charcoal grey, and soon it was raining heavily.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_CocoMaya_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_CocoMaya_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Angel likes to tell the story about how one Labor Day in
         <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/46/">
          Cape May
         </a>
         , I was so determined to soak up the last  few hours of summer sun that I stubbornly refused to leave the beach, despite the day's gale-force winds.  He tried to stick it out with me but finally, his mouth full of sand and his eyes full of grit, he had no choice but to leave me there.  When he returned a few hours later, only the edge of my blanket, the corner of my magazine, and a few strands of blonde hair were visible beneath a wind-swept, Tracey-shaped mound of sand.
        </p>
        <p>
         That was me with that swing as soon as it started to rain.  I knew that if I didn't move, I was going to get soaked.  I knew I would be cold and damp later, particularly on the air-conditioned ferry (and that somehow it would be Angel's fault).  And I knew from experience that running around in wet flip-flops is the safety equivalent of running around with both legs stuffed into one pant leg.  But I also knew that I had the best damn bar seat in the universe, and no tropical depression was going to get me to move.
        </p>
        <p>
         Eventually, though, the rain became so heavy that I knew we'd better make a run for the car before it floated away.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CocoMaya_24.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CocoMaya_24.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_van_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_van_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CocoMaya_26.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CocoMaya_26.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Although I felt bad for this driver, I was immensely relieved that that tree didn't land on
         <em>
          our
         </em>
         car.  After the false-alarm calls to the rental company about the keys earlier that day, a call informing them that we could not return the car because there was a tree on top of it surely would have landed me on yet another blacklist.
        </p>
        <p>
         That night marked the first of three reservations I'd made back on Tortola at The Dove, a tiny jewel-box of a restaurant housed inside an historic West Indian cottage near the waterfront in Road Town.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DoveInt_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DoveInt_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         I guess the fact that I started emailing them back in September and made three reservations over the course of a nine-night visit made an impression, because when I gave the hostess my last name she exclaimed, "Oh, you're
         <em>
          Tracey
         </em>
         !  We've been expecting you!"  Which translates to, "We doubled our usual food order this week, just to be safe."
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DoveInt_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DoveInt_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DoveInt_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DoveInt_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DoveInt_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DoveInt_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The Dove had been one of the highlights of our trip six years ago, and we were delighted to find that virtually nothing had changed since our last visit: The restaurant was still cozy and candlelit, with warm red walls, comfy banquettes strewn with satin pillows, and a glimmering chandelier.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DoveInt_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DoveInt_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DoveInt_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DoveInt_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DoveInt_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DoveInt_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_WindowRedo_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_WindowRedo_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Since our last visit, however, they've added a funky outdoor patio, the centerpiece of which is a mango tree aglow in flickering candles, along with a comfortable lounge area for nibbling appetizers and sipping Champagne.  That's right, Champagne.  From
         <em>
          France
         </em>
         .  I told you this trip was going to be luxurious,
         <em>
          n'est-ce pas
         </em>
         ?
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_DoveInt_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_DoveInt_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DoveInt_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DoveInt_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DoveInt_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DoveInt_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_DoveInt_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_DoveInt_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         For dinner that evening, we each started with a bowl of spicy coconut lobster bisque with cumin-roasted almonds, cilantro, and lime creme fraiche, followed by the seafood melange for Angel, which was overflowing with cod, clams, shrimp, scallops, squid, and chorizo, and swimming in a rich, Chardonnay-and-tomato broth perfumed with saffron.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_Dove1_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_Dove1_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_Dove1_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_Dove1_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_Dove1_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_Dove1_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         I decided on the mushroom and leek risotto, which had a lovely bit of "crunch" to it thanks to a celery-walnut ragout . . . and a fried egg yolk on top.  Those delicious little cholesterol bombs ought to come with a warning: Don't try this at home . . . unless your life insurance is up-to-date.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_Dove1_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_Dove1_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Throw in an icy bottle of Sancerre with just enough left after dinner for a nightcap outside on the patio, and The Dove easily held on to its place at the top of our must-do dining list in Tortola.
        </p>
        <p>
         But really, they had me at fried egg yolks.
        </p>
        <p>
         The next day was Christmas.  Although we had agreed not to bring any gifts with us to save room for more important stuff in our luggage, like hair dryers and ironing boards, Angel not only broke our agreement, but got me one of the best Christmas presents of all time.   You see, my sister Trina has exquisite taste, particularly with respect to home dcor and apparel.  Over the years I have been so enamored of various items in her possession  everything from candleholders and beach cover-ups to dishtowels, sweaters, and even a reclaimed radiator cover that she cleverly refurbished  that she frequently jokes that she hides all of her best stuff when I come around, for fear that I will stamp it with my name and take it home with me.  And so, Quick, hide that before Tracey gets her stamper! is as common a phrase when I am around as, Wait, you ate
         <em>
          all
         </em>
         of it?
        </p>
        <p>
         Which is why Angel got me this for Christmas.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_Stamper_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_Stamper_1.jpg"/>
         <br/>
         <img alt="thumb_2013_BVI_Stamper_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/thumb_2013_BVI_Stamper_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Forget that old saw about a good spouse being one who knows everything about you and likes you anyway.  What you really want is a spouse who not only tolerates your worst habits, but actually
         <em>
          facilitates
         </em>
         them.
        </p>
        <p>
         After a quick swim and a short visit with the sleepy Bella, it was time to begin the day.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_XmasDrive_25.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_XmasDrive_25.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_Animals_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_Animals_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Little did we know that it would end in a hail of obscenities and (squirt) gun fire.
         <br/>
         -----------------------------------------------------
         <br/>
         <a class="enlarge_image" href="/image_enlarge.cfm?src=http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_Dove1_6.jpg" onclick="raw_popup(this);return false" title="Click for full size image">
          <img alt="2013_BVI_Dove1_6.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/thumb_2013_BVI_Dove1_6.jpg"/>
         </a>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="entrydetails">
        Posted by
        <a href="/author/293321/">
         TraceyG
        </a>
        <a class="entry_link" href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/90/">
         06:22
        </a>
        <span class="country_links">
         Archived in
         <a class="country_link" href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/co/222/" rel="nofollow">
          British Virgin Islands
         </a>
        </span>
        <span class="tag_links">

      <div class="entry">
       <h2 class="entrytitle" id="Entry92">
        <a href="http://traceyg.travellerspoint.com/92/" rel="bookmark" title="Permanent link to The BVIs, Part 3: Merry Christmas, Ya Filthy Animal ">
         The BVIs, Part 3: Merry Christmas, Ya Filthy Animal
        </a>
       </h2>
       <p class="preentrydetails">
        <span class="entrydate">
         01.28.2014
        </span>
       </p>
       <div class="entrycontent">
        <p>
         It was now Christmas Day, and I'd naturally made our lunch plans well in advance.  I decided on the Lambert Beach Resort, an out-of-the-way property at the far eastern end of Tortola, and through a series of emails I was assured that they were most definitely open for lunch on Christmas and that no reservation was necessary and that they looked forward to seeing us.   And so on Christmas morning we set off for the other end of the island, taking the longer but more scenic Ridge Road, which runs along the island's mountainous spine.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_MtHouse_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_MtHouse_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_XmasDrive_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_XmasDrive_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_XmasDrive_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_XmasDrive_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         For the first hour or so, we ascended higher and higher up the mountain, stopping frequently for photos.  Although the day was hazy, the views became more and more spectacular.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_XmasDrive_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_XmasDrive_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_XmasDrive_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_XmasDrive_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_XmasDrive_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_XmasDrive_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_XmasDrive_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_XmasDrive_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_XmasDrive_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_XmasDrive_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Along the way we encountered donkeys, cows, and other animals, almost none of whom were happy to be having their photo taken . . . and were not shy about saying so.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_Animals_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_Animals_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_Animals_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_Animals_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_Animals_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_Animals_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Well, except this guy.  Then again, if he knew how many of his brethren I've gobbled up over the years, he probably would've told me to get lost, too.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_XmasDrive_22.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_XmasDrive_22.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The route soon became slow and arduous, repeatedly requiring us to scale the mountain via a series of angled switchbacks; slowly and carefully descend back down; then climb right back up again in order to go . . . straight ahead.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_XmasDrive_18.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_XmasDrive_18.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_XmasDrive_20.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_XmasDrive_20.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_XmasDrive_21.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_XmasDrive_21.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         By the second hour, we both had to pee and were getting hungry.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_XmasDrive_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_XmasDrive_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_HouseFence_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_HouseFence_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         As we neared the three-hour mark, I was kicking myself for not packing a jar of emergency peanut butter.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_XmasDrive_24.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_XmasDrive_24.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Finally, a Christmas miracle -- a sign directing us to Lambert Beach Resort!  We attempted to gun the engine up the final series of steep hills -- the Tortolan equivalent of a marathoner crawling across the finish line and then promptly throwing up -- and, at long last, we pulled into the parking lot at Lambert Beach Resort, nearly three hours after we'd left the house.  We were tired, hungry, and in urgent need of both a bathroom and a cocktail.
        </p>
        <p>
         But both of those could wait because . . . kittens!!!
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_LambertCats_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_LambertCats_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_LambertCats_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_LambertCats_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_LambertCats_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_LambertCats_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_LambertCats_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_LambertCats_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_CatLeaf_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_CatLeaf_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Eventually I tore myself away and we made our way over to the restaurant.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_Lambert_7.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_Lambert_7.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_Lambert_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_Lambert_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The restaurant was completely empty.  I don't just mean that the 11:30 people never showed.  I mean
         <em>
          empty
         </em>
         : No table settings. No menus. No bottles or glassware behind the bar.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_Lambert_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_Lambert_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         And no people, save for a lone woman sitting at one of the tables using her computer.  She gamely explained that the waitstaff had all gone home and the chef was at the beach, and therefore there hadn't been any food or drink at the resort for the past several days.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_Lambert_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_Lambert_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         She also genially offered to make us sandwiches in her room, which we politely declined (though not without some regret on my part).  Later, while we explained to the disinterested woman from the front desk that this whole fiasco was completely unacceptable, Sandwich Lady helpfully piped up, "Oh, you should have been here last year.  It was even worse!"
        </p>
        <p>
         (Wait a minute.  You spent last year's vacation at a resort with
         <em>
          no food or drinks
         </em>
         , and then you came BACK the following year?!?!   I have some swampland in Florida that we should talk about.)
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_Lambert_6.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_Lambert_6.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Now, if you have been reading this blog for any length of time, you know that I like to eat.  And I eat way more, and way more often, than the average person.  And so, when it finally became clear that we had driven almost three hours LITERALLY UPHILL BOTH WAYS to get to Lambert Beach Resort for lunch, and that there was not actually going to
         <em>
          be
         </em>
         any lunch, well . . . I lost it.  And it is particularly fitting that I lost it on Christmas Day, because the only way to explain what happened next is to use an example from one of the most famous Christmas movies of all time, "A Christmas Story."  You know the scene: Young Ralphie, having been tormented for weeks by the neighborhood bully Scut Farkus, finally snaps and beats the living crap out of him, all while uttering a string of unmentionable curse words.  In a voice-over, adult Ralphie explains: "I have since heard of people under extreme duress speaking in strange tongues. I became conscious that a steady torrent of obscenities and swearing of all kinds was pouring out of me as I screamed."
        </p>
        <p>
         There were no beatings that day at the Lambert Beach Resort -- it was Christmas, after all -- but there was most certainly a steady torrent of obscenities and swearing of all kinds when I found out that I wasn't going to get my lunch.
        </p>
        <p>
         (I wish I could say that we jumped in the car, revved the engine, and left skid marks on our way out of there, but the 90-degree hill we had to chug up to leave the parking lot didn't really allow for a dramatic exit.  It was like trying to stomp out of a tent.)
        </p>
        <p>
         After about another hour of driving, we made a fortuitous wrong turn in Road Town and ended up at the Village Cay Marina, a spot that we both vaguely remembered from six years ago as the site where we crashed a wedding after one too many bottles of wine at The Dove.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_VillageCay_2.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_VillageCay_2.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_VillageCay_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_VillageCay_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Thank you, Village Cay, for operating a restaurant with actual food.  Your chicken fingers were juicy and tender, your shrimp wrap was overstuffed and tasty, and I am grateful that your bar was open so I did not have to go all "Roadhouse" on you.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_VillageCay_3.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_VillageCay_3.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_VillageCay_4.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_VillageCay_4.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_VillageCay_5.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_VillageCay_5.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_VillageCay_6.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_VillageCay_6.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Right nearby is the quaint and colorful Crafts Alive outdoor market, where I put that new stamper of mine to good use.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CraftsAlive_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CraftsAlive_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CraftsAlive_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CraftsAlive_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CraftsAlive_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CraftsAlive_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CraftsAlive_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CraftsAlive_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CraftsAlive_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CraftsAlive_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CraftsAlive_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CraftsAlive_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CraftsAlive_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CraftsAlive_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_CraftRedo_1.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_CraftRedo_1.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CraftsAlive_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CraftsAlive_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_CraftsAlive_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_CraftsAlive_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Back at Peach Cottage, we took a quick nap, then got ready for our dinner reservation at the Sugar Mill Hotel, whose lovely restaurant is housed in a romantic 17th century sugar mill with the original stone walls and beamed ceilings.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_SugarMill_15.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_SugarMill_15.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_SugarMill_02.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_SugarMill_02.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_SugarMill_01.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_SugarMill_01.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The Sugar Mill was one of several restaurants we visited on this trip that indulged us in the charming British tradition of the "Christmas Cracker," a brightly colored tube that's twisted at both ends.  The cracker makes a popping sound when pulled apart, and inside you'll typically find a small token gift, a joke, and (best of all!) a shiny paper crown.  We'd received utilitarian gifts like a tape measure and a shoe horn in the crackers at other restaurants, but the Sugar Mill must have known I was coming, because Angel received a
         <a class="external" href="http://www.amazon.com/144-Fortune-Teller-Miracle-Fish/dp/B000OF0EY8" title="This is an external link">
          mood fish
         </a>
         and I received . . . a miniature pink squirt gun!!!  You probably don't need a mood fish to guess Angel's mood from that moment on.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_SugarMill_03.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_SugarMill_03.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_SugarMill_16.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_SugarMill_16.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_SugarMill_04.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_SugarMill_04.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_SugarMill_05.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_SugarMill_05.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Dinner was fantastic, with pumpkin-and-black-bean soup for Angel, tuna tartare for me, and an un-ordered salad course for both of us.  Extra food: Merry Christmas to me!
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_SugarMill_06.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_SugarMill_06.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_SugarMill_07.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_SugarMill_07.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_SugarMill_08.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_SugarMill_08.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Angel barely even looked at the menu before deciding on the traditional turkey dinner, while I settled on the lobster medallions with risotto.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_SugarMill_11.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_SugarMill_11.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_SugarMill_10.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_SugarMill_10.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_SugarMill_09.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_SugarMill_09.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="2013_BVI_SugarMill_12.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/2013_BVI_SugarMill_12.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_SugarMill_13.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_SugarMill_13.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         We each ordered the apple pie for dessert, which was the only disappointing note of the meal because it was served cold.  So we took it to go, warmed it up back at the house, and ate it in bed.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="large_2013_BVI_SugarMill_14.jpg" class="photo" src="http://photos.travellerspoint.com/293321/large_2013_BVI_SugarMill_14.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         That's one way to salvage Lunchless Christmas.
         <br/>
         -------------------------------------------------------------------
         <br/>
         <em>
          Next up, a day trip to Jost Van Dyke, where the beaches will be beautiful, the Painkillers will be plentiful, and the restaurant will be open . . . or "Boxing Day" will take on a whole new meaning.
         </em>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="entrydetails">
